using CafebookModel.Model.ModelWeb.KhachHang;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using System.Security.Claims;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Account
{
    [Authorize(Roles = "KhachHang")]
    public class ThongTinCaNhanModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;

        [BindProperty]
        public ThongTinCaNhanUpdateDto Input { get; set; } = new();

        [BindProperty]
        public IFormFile? AvatarFile { get; set; }

        public string AvatarHienTaiUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public bool IsEditMode { get; set; } = false;

        public ThongTinCaNhanModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        private int GetCurrentUserId()
        {
            var userIdClaim = User.FindFirstValue(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier);
            int.TryParse(userIdClaim, out int userId);
            return userId;
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnGetAsync(string? handler)
        {
            var userId = GetCurrentUserId();
            if (userId == 0)
            {
                await HttpContext.SignOutAsync();
                return RedirectToPage("/Account/DangNhapView");
            }

            if (handler == "Edit") IsEditMode = true;

            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            try
            {
                var response = await httpClient.GetAsync($"api/web/khachhang/thongtincanhan/{userId}");

                if (response.StatusCode == System.Net.HttpStatusCode.Unauthorized)
                {
                    await HttpContext.SignOutAsync();
                    return RedirectToPage("/Account/DangNhapView");
                }

                if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                {
                    var profile = await response.Content.ReadFromJsonAsync<ThongTinCaNhanDto>();
                    if (profile != null)
                    {
                        Input.HoTen = profile.HoTen;
                        Input.SoDienThoai = profile.SoDienThoai;
                        Input.Email = profile.Email;
                        Input.DiaChi = profile.DiaChi;
                        Input.TenDangNhap = profile.TenDangNhap ?? "";
                        string cleanUrl = profile.AnhDaiDienUrl.Split('?')[0]; 
                        AvatarHienTaiUrl = cleanUrl + "?v=" + DateTime.Now.Ticks;
                        HttpContext.Session.SetString("AvatarUrl", AvatarHienTaiUrl);
                    }
                    return Page();
                }
                else
                {
                    TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Không thể tải dữ liệu hồ sơ. Vui lòng thử lại sau.";
                    return Page();
                }
            }
            catch (Exception)
            {
                TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Không thể kết nối đến máy chủ API.";
                return Page();
            }
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostAsync()
        {
            var userId = GetCurrentUserId();
            if (userId == 0)
            {
                await HttpContext.SignOutAsync();
                return RedirectToPage("/Account/DangNhapView");
            }

            if (!ModelState.IsValid) return await OnGetAsync("Edit");

            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            using var formData = new MultipartFormDataContent();

            formData.Add(new StringContent(Input.HoTen), nameof(Input.HoTen));
            formData.Add(new StringContent(Input.SoDienThoai ?? ""), nameof(Input.SoDienThoai));
            formData.Add(new StringContent(Input.Email ?? ""), nameof(Input.Email));
            formData.Add(new StringContent(Input.DiaChi ?? ""), nameof(Input.DiaChi));
            formData.Add(new StringContent(Input.TenDangNhap), nameof(Input.TenDangNhap));

            if (AvatarFile != null)
            {
                formData.Add(new StreamContent(AvatarFile.OpenReadStream()), "avatarFile", AvatarFile.FileName);
            }

            try
            {
                var response = await httpClient.PutAsync($"api/web/khachhang/thongtincanhan/update/{userId}", formData);

                if (response.StatusCode == System.Net.HttpStatusCode.Unauthorized)
                {
                    await HttpContext.SignOutAsync();
                    return RedirectToPage("/Account/DangNhapView");
                }

                if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                {
                    TempData["SuccessMessage"] = "Cập nhật hồ sơ thành công!";
                    var result = await response.Content.ReadFromJsonAsync<UpdateResponse>();

                    await UpdateClaims(Input.HoTen, Input.TenDangNhap);
                    return RedirectToPage();
                }
                else
                {
                    ModelState.AddModelError(string.Empty, "Cập nhật thất bại. Vui lòng kiểm tra lại dữ liệu.");
                    AvatarHienTaiUrl = HttpContext.Session.GetString("AvatarUrl") ?? "";
                    IsEditMode = true;
                    return Page();
                }
            }
            catch (Exception)
            {
                TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Lỗi hệ thống khi cập nhật.";
                return await OnGetAsync("Edit");
            }
        }

        private async Task UpdateClaims(string newHoTen, string newTenDangNhap)
        {
            var user = User.Identity as ClaimsIdentity;
            if (user != null)
            {
                var oldGivenName = user.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.GivenName);
                if (oldGivenName != null) user.RemoveClaim(oldGivenName);
                user.AddClaim(new Claim(ClaimTypes.GivenName, newHoTen));

                var oldName = user.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.Name);
                if (oldName != null) user.RemoveClaim(oldName);
                user.AddClaim(new Claim(ClaimTypes.Name, newTenDangNhap));

                await HttpContext.SignOutAsync();
                await HttpContext.SignInAsync(new ClaimsPrincipal(user));
            }
        }

        private class UpdateResponse { public string newAvatarUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty; }
    }
}

            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
                let timeLeft = 60;
                let countdownTimer;
                const btnResend = document.getElementById('btnResendOtp');
        
                function startCountdown() {
                    timeLeft = 60;
                    btnResend.disabled = true;
                    btnResend.style.color = '#9E9E9E'; 
                    btnResend.innerHTML = `Gửi lại mã (<span id="otpCountdown">${timeLeft}</span>s)`;

                    countdownTimer = setInterval(() => {
                        timeLeft--;
                        document.getElementById('otpCountdown').innerText = timeLeft;

                        if (timeLeft <= 0) {
                            clearInterval(countdownTimer);
                            btnResend.disabled = false;
                            btnResend.style.color = '#D84315'; 
                            btnResend.innerHTML = 'Gửi lại mã ngay';
                        }
                    }, 1000);
                }

                startCountdown();

                btnResend.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    if (!this.disabled) {
                        alert("Yêu cầu gửi lại mã đã được thực thi!");
                
                        startCountdown();
                                    }
                });
            });
    </script>

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using CafebookModel.Model.ModelWeb.KhachHang;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Account
{
    public class XacMinhOtpViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        public XacMinhOtpViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory) => _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;

        [BindProperty] public OtpInputModel Input { get; set; } = new();
        public string? ReturnUrl { get; set; }

        [TempData] public string? OtpMessage { get; set; }

        public class OtpInputModel
        {
            public int TempId { get; set; }
            public string TempPassword { get; set; } = string.Empty;
            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập mã OTP")] public string OtpCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;
            [Required] public string EditableEmail { get; set; } = string.Empty;
            [Required] public string EditablePhone { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet(string? returnUrl = null)
        {
            // Bắt buộc phải có TempId từ trang Đăng Ký chuyển qua
            if (TempData["TempId"] == null) return RedirectToPage("/Account/DangKyView");

            ReturnUrl = returnUrl;

            // Lấy dữ liệu đẩy xuống giao diện
            Input.TempId = Convert.ToInt32(TempData["TempId"]);
            Input.TempPassword = TempData["TempPassword"]?.ToString() ?? "";
            Input.EditableEmail = TempData["TempEmail"]?.ToString() ?? "";
            Input.EditablePhone = TempData["TempPhone"]?.ToString() ?? "";

            // Lấy Message để hiển thị, TempData tự Keep nhờ thuộc tính [TempData] ở trên
            OtpMessage = TempData["OtpMessage"]?.ToString();

            return Page();
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostAsync(string? returnUrl = null)
        {
            returnUrl ??= Url.Content("~/");
            if (!ModelState.IsValid) return Page();

            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            var apiRequest = new VerifyOtpRequestDto
            {
                TempId = Input.TempId,
                Email = Input.EditableEmail,
                SoDienThoai = Input.EditablePhone,
                Password = Input.TempPassword,
                OtpCode = Input.OtpCode
            };

            var response = await httpClient.PostAsJsonAsync("api/web/khachhang/dangky/verify-otp", apiRequest);
            if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var apiResponse = await response.Content.ReadFromJsonAsync<DangKyResponseDto>();
                if (apiResponse != null && apiResponse.Success)
                {
                    // XÁC THỰC XONG -> VỀ ĐĂNG NHẬP
                    TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Xác thực thành công! Tài khoản đã được kích hoạt. Vui lòng đăng nhập.";
                    return RedirectToPage("/Account/DangNhapView", new { returnUrl = returnUrl });
                }
                ModelState.AddModelError(string.Empty, apiResponse?.Message ?? "Mã OTP không đúng hoặc đã hết hạn.");
            }
            return Page();
        }
    }
}

﻿using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Caching.Memory;
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Account // SỬA: Namespace
{
    public class XacNhanMaViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IMemoryCache _cache;

        public XacNhanMaViewModel(IMemoryCache cache)
        {
            _cache = cache;
        }

        [BindProperty]
        public InputModel Input { get; set; } = new InputModel();

        [TempData]
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; set; }

        public class InputModel
        {
            [Required]
            [HiddenInput]
            public string Email { get; set; } = string.Empty;

            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập mã xác nhận.")]
            [Display(Name = "Mã Xác Nhận")]
            [RegularExpression(@"^\d{6}$", ErrorMessage = "Mã xác nhận phải gồm 6 chữ số.")]
            public string VerificationCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet()
        {
            var email = TempData["VerificationEmail"] as string;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(email))
            {
                return RedirectToPage("./QuenMatKhauView");
            }

            Input.Email = email;
            TempData.Keep("VerificationEmail");
            return Page();
        }

        public IActionResult OnPostAsync()
        {
            if (!ModelState.IsValid)
            {
                return Page();
            }

            string email = Input.Email;
            string cacheKey = $"ForgotPassword_{email}";

            if (_cache.TryGetValue(cacheKey, out string? cachedCode))
            {
                if (cachedCode == Input.VerificationCode)
                {
                    // Mã ĐÚNG. Tạo token reset
                    string resetToken = Guid.NewGuid().ToString("N");
                    string resetCacheKey = $"ResetToken_{email}";
                    var resetCacheOptions = new MemoryCacheEntryOptions()
                        .SetAbsoluteExpiration(TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10));

                    _cache.Set(resetCacheKey, resetToken, resetCacheOptions);
                    _cache.Remove(cacheKey);
                    TempData.Remove("VerificationEmail");

                    return RedirectToPage("./DatLaiMatKhauView", new { email = email, token = resetToken });
                }
                else
                {
                    ErrorMessage = "Mã xác nhận không đúng.";
                    TempData.Keep("VerificationEmail");
                    return Page();
                }
            }
            else
            {
                ErrorMessage = "Mã xác nhận đã hết hạn hoặc không tồn tại.";
                TempData.Keep("VerificationEmail");
                return Page();
            }
        }
    }
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";
        let _config = null;
        let _currentData = [];
        let _currentMode = 'list';

        const _daysMap = {
            2: "Thứ Hai", 3: "Thứ Ba", 4: "Thứ Tư", 5: "Thứ Năm",
            6: "Thứ Sáu", 7: "Thứ Bảy", 8: "Chủ Nhật"
        };

        function getMonday(d) {
            d = new Date(d);
            var day = d.getDay(), diff = d.getDate() - day + (day === 0 ? -6 : 1);
            return new Date(d.setDate(diff));
        }

        async function init() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/config`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
                if(res.ok) _config = await res.json();
            } catch(e) { console.error("Lỗi lấy config", e); }

            const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
            $("#date-filter").val(today);
            loadData(today);
        }

        async function loadData(selectedDate) {
            const monday = getMonday(selectedDate);
            const mondayStr = monday.toISOString().split('T')[0];

            $("#list-body, #my-list-body").html('<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center py-5"><div class="spinner-border" style="color: var(--dkl-primary)"></div></td></tr>');
            $("#kanban-board").html('<div class="text-center py-5 w-100"><div class="spinner-border" style="color: var(--dkl-primary)"></div></div>');
            
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/weekly-shifts?monday=${mondayStr}`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` }, cache: 'no-store' });
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Lỗi tải dữ liệu");
                _currentData = await response.json();
                renderUI();
            } catch (error) {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Không thể tải dữ liệu.', 'error');
            }
        }

        function renderUI() {
            const selDate = $("#date-filter").val();
            renderMyShifts(_currentData.filter(x => x.trangThaiCuaToi !== 'Chưa đăng ký'));
                        if (_currentMode === 'list') {
                const dayData = _currentData.filter(x => x.trangThaiCuaToi === 'Chưa đăng ký' && x.ngayLam.startsWith(selDate));
                renderList(dayData);
            } else {
                const weekData = _currentData.filter(x => x.trangThaiCuaToi === 'Chưa đăng ký');
                renderKanban(weekData, getMonday(selDate));
            }
        }

        function renderList(data) {
            const $body = $("#list-body").empty();
            if(data.length === 0) return $body.append('<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center py-5 text-muted fst-italic"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 mb-2">event_busy</span><br/>Không có ca trống trong ngày này.</td></tr>');
            
            data.forEach((s, i) => {
                const delay = (i % 10) * 0.05;
                const dateFormatted = new Date(s.ngayLam).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN', { weekday: 'short', day: '2-digit', month: '2-digit' });
                let statusBadge = '', actionBtn = '';

                if (s.isQuaHan) {
                    statusBadge = '<span class="badge bg-secondary-subtle text-secondary border px-3 py-2 rounded-pill">Đã qua giờ</span>';
                    actionBtn = '<button class="btn btn-light btn-sm rounded-pill px-4 text-muted" disabled>Khóa</button>';
                } else if (s.soLuongDaDangKy >= s.soLuongCan) {
                    statusBadge = '<span class="badge bg-danger-subtle text-danger border px-3 py-2 rounded-pill">Đã đủ người</span>';
                    actionBtn = '<button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm rounded-pill px-4" disabled>Đã chốt</button>';
                } else {
                    statusBadge = `<span class="badge bg-success-subtle text-success border px-3 py-2 rounded-pill"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">person_add</span> Cần thêm ${s.soLuongCan - s.soLuongDaDangKy}</span>`;
                    actionBtn = `<button class="btn btn-primary-coffee btn-sm rounded-pill px-4 fw-bold shadow-sm" onclick="registerShift(${s.idNhuCau}, '${s.tenCa}')">Đăng ký ngay</button>`;
                }

                $body.append(`
                    <tr class="anim-item ${s.isQuaHan ? 'opacity-50' : ''}" style="animation-delay: ${delay}s">
                        <td class="ps-4 fw-bold text-dark"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle text-muted">calendar_today</span> ${dateFormatted}</td>
                        <td>
                            <div class="fw-bold text-dark" style="color: var(--dkl-primary) !important;">${s.tenCa}</div>
                            <div class="small text-muted"><span class="material-symbols-outlined" style="font-size: 14px; vertical-align: text-bottom;">schedule</span> ${s.gioBatDau.substring(0,5)} - ${s.gioKetThuc.substring(0,5)}</div>
                            ${s.ghiChu ? `<div class="small mt-1"><span class="badge bg-warning-subtle text-dark border-warning-subtle"><span class="material-symbols-outlined" style="font-size: 12px">campaign</span> ${s.ghiChu}</span></div>` : ''}
                        </td>
                        <td><div class="fw-bold text-dark fs-6">${s.soLuongDaDangKy} <span class="text-muted fw-normal">/ ${s.soLuongCan}</span></div></td>
                        <td>${statusBadge}</td>
                        <td class="text-center pe-4">${actionBtn}</td>
                    </tr>
                `);
            });
        }

        function renderKanban(data, monday) {
            const $board = $("#kanban-board").empty();
            if(!_config) return;

            _config.thuMoCua.forEach((dayNum, i) => {
                let offset = dayNum === 8 ? 6 : dayNum - 2;
                let colDate = new Date(monday);
                colDate.setDate(monday.getDate() + offset);
                let dateStr = colDate.toISOString().split('T')[0];
                
                let shiftsForDay = data.filter(d => d.ngayLam.startsWith(dateStr));
                let isToday = (dateStr === new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]);

                let $col = $(`
                    <div class="dkl-column anim-item ${isToday ? 'today-col' : ''}" style="animation-delay: ${i*0.05}s">
                        <div class="dkl-col-header">
                            <div class="fw-bold text-uppercase fs-5 mb-1" style="color: var(--dkl-primary)">${_daysMap[dayNum]}</div>
                            <div class="small fw-medium text-muted">${colDate.toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="dkl-col-body"></div>
                    </div>
                `);
                
                let $body = $col.find(".dkl-col-body");

                if(shiftsForDay.length === 0) {
                    $body.append('<div class="text-center text-muted small mt-5 fst-italic">Không có ca</div>');
                } else {
                    shiftsForDay.forEach(s => {
                        let isFull = s.soLuongDaDangKy >= s.soLuongCan;
                        let cClass = s.isQuaHan ? "card-expired" : (isFull ? "card-full" : "card-available");
                        let sBadge = s.isQuaHan ? `<span class="badge bg-secondary-subtle text-secondary w-100 py-2">Đã qua giờ</span>` : (isFull ? `<span class="badge bg-danger-subtle text-danger w-100 py-2">Đã chốt đủ</span>` : `<span class="badge bg-success-subtle text-success w-100 py-2">Tuyển thêm ${s.soLuongCan - s.soLuongDaDangKy}</span>`);
                        let aBtn = (s.isQuaHan || isFull) ? '' : `<button type="button" class="btn btn-primary-coffee btn-sm w-100 mt-2 fw-bold rounded-pill" onclick="registerShift(${s.idNhuCau}, '${s.tenCa}')">Đăng Ký</button>`;

                        $body.append(`
                            <div class="dkl-card ${cClass}">
                                <div class="fw-bold fs-6 mb-1" style="color: var(--dkl-primary)">${s.tenCa}</div>
                                <div class="small text-muted mb-2 fw-medium d-flex align-items-center gap-1">
                                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6">schedule</span> ${s.gioBatDau.substring(0,5)} - ${s.gioKetThuc.substring(0,5)}
                                </div>
                                ${sBadge}
                                ${aBtn}
                            </div>
                        `);
                    });
                }
                $board.append($col);
            });
        }

        function renderMyShifts(data) {
            const $body = $("#my-list-body").empty();
            if(data.length === 0) return $body.append('<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center py-5 text-muted fst-italic"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 mb-2">pending_actions</span><br/>Bạn chưa đăng ký ca nào trong tuần này.</td></tr>');
            
            data.forEach((s, i) => {
                const delay = (i % 10) * 0.05;
                const dateFormatted = new Date(s.ngayLam).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN', { weekday: 'short', day: '2-digit', month: '2-digit' });
                let badge = s.trangThaiCuaToi === 'Chờ duyệt'
                    ? '<span class="badge bg-warning-subtle text-warning border border-warning-subtle px-3 py-2 rounded-pill"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">hourglass_empty</span> Chờ quản lý duyệt</span>'
                    : '<span class="badge bg-success-subtle text-success border border-success-subtle px-3 py-2 rounded-pill"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">check_circle</span> Lịch chính thức</span>';
                
                let actionBtn = s.trangThaiCuaToi === 'Chờ duyệt'
                    ? `<button type="button" class="btn btn-outline-danger btn-sm rounded-pill px-3 d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center mx-auto gap-1" onclick="cancelShift(${s.idLichCuaToi})"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6">close</span> Hủy ca</button>`
                    : '<span class="text-muted small fst-italic"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">lock</span> Không thể hủy</span>';

                $body.append(`
                    <tr class="anim-item" style="animation-delay: ${delay}s">
                        <td class="ps-4 fw-bold text-dark"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle text-muted">calendar_today</span> ${dateFormatted}</td>
                        <td>
                            <div class="fw-bold" style="color: var(--dkl-primary)">${s.tenCa}</div>
                            <div class="small text-muted"><span class="material-symbols-outlined" style="font-size: 14px; vertical-align: text-bottom;">schedule</span> ${s.gioBatDau.substring(0,5)} - ${s.gioKetThuc.substring(0,5)}</div>
                        </td>
                        <td>${s.ghiChuCuaToi ? `<span class="badge bg-light text-dark text-wrap text-start border p-2 rounded-3"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle text-accent">push_pin</span> ${s.ghiChuCuaToi}</span>` : '<span class="text-muted small fst-italic">-- Không có --</span>'}</td>
                        <td>${badge}</td>
                        <td class="text-center pe-4">${actionBtn}</td>
                    </tr>
                `);
            });
        }

        async function registerShift(idNhuCau, tenCa) {
            const { value: note } = await Swal.fire({
                title: `Đăng ký ${tenCa}`,
                input: 'text',
                inputLabel: 'Bạn muốn ứng tuyển vị trí nào? (VD: Thu ngân, Phục vụ...)',
                inputPlaceholder: 'Ghi chú cho quản lý...',
                showCancelButton: true,
                confirmButtonText: 'Xác nhận Đăng ký',
                cancelButtonText: 'Đóng',
                confirmButtonColor: '#5D4037' // Màu Theme
            });
            if (note !== undefined) {
                try {
                    const response = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/register`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                        body: JSON.stringify({ idNhuCau, ghiChuNhanVien: note })
                    });
                    if (response.ok) {
                        Swal.fire({ title: 'Thành công', text: 'Yêu cầu đã được gửi đến Quản lý.', icon: 'success', timer: 2000, showConfirmButton: false });
                        loadData($("#date-filter").val());
                        var tab = new bootstrap.Tab(document.querySelector('#my-tab'));
                        tab.show();
                    } else {
                        let msg = "Lỗi.";
                        try { const err = await response.json(); msg = err.message || msg; } catch(e) {}
                        Swal.fire('Không thể đăng ký', msg, 'warning');
                    }
                } catch (error) { Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Mất kết nối máy chủ', 'error'); }
            }
        }

        async function cancelShift(idLich) {
            if ((await Swal.fire({title: 'Hủy đăng ký?', text: "Rút lại yêu cầu đăng ký ca làm này?", icon: 'warning', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#D32F2F', confirmButtonText: 'Hủy'})).isConfirmed) {
                const response = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/cancel/${idLich}`, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
                if (response.ok) {
                    Swal.fire({ title: 'Đã hủy', icon: 'success', timer: 1000, showConfirmButton: false });
                    loadData($("#date-filter").val());
                } else {
                    let msg = "Lỗi.";
                    try { const err = await response.json(); msg = err.message || msg; } catch(e) {}
                    Swal.fire('Lỗi', msg, 'error');
                }
            }
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
            // Chuyển Mode List / Kanban
            $("input[name='vbtn-radio']").change(function() {
                _currentMode = this.id === 'viewKanban' ? 'kanban' : 'list';
                if(_currentMode === 'kanban') { $("#mode-list").addClass("d-none"); $("#mode-kanban").removeClass("d-none"); }
                else { $("#mode-kanban").addClass("d-none"); $("#mode-list").removeClass("d-none"); }
                renderUI();
            });

            // Thay đổi Ngày/Tuần
            $("#date-filter").on("change", function() { loadData($(this).val()); });
            
            $("#btnPrev").click(function() {
                let d = new Date($("#date-filter").val());
                d.setDate(d.getDate() - (_currentMode === 'list' ? 1 : 7));
                $("#date-filter").val(d.toISOString().split('T')[0]).trigger('change');
            });
            
            $("#btnNext").click(function() {
                let d = new Date($("#date-filter").val());
                d.setDate(d.getDate() + (_currentMode === 'list' ? 1 : 7));
                $("#date-filter").val(d.toISOString().split('T')[0]).trigger('change');
            });

            init();
        });
    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class DangKyLichViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public DangKyLichViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet()
        {
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken))
            {
                string currentUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString;
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = currentUrl });
            }

            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/dangkylichweb";

            return Page();
        }
    }
}

================================================================================
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System.Security.Claims;
using CafebookModel.Model.Shared;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication.Cookies;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using System.Text.Json;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [IgnoreAntiforgeryToken]
    public class DangNhapEmployeeModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        public DangNhapEmployeeModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        [BindProperty]
        public InputModel Input { get; set; } = new();

        [TempData]
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; set; }

        public string? ReturnUrl { get; set; }

        public class InputModel
        {
            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập Tên đăng nhập, Email hoặc SĐT")]
            public string TenDangNhap { get; set; } = string.Empty;

            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập mật khẩu")]
            [DataType(DataType.Password)]
            public string MatKhau { get; set; } = string.Empty;

            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập mã xác thực")]
            public string CaptchaResult { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        }

        private void GenerateCaptcha()
        {
            const string chars = "ABCDEFGHJKLMNPQRSTUVWXYZ23456789";
            var random = new Random();
            var captcha = new string(Enumerable.Repeat(chars, 5)
                .Select(s => s[random.Next(s.Length)]).ToArray());

            HttpContext.Session.SetString("CaptchaCode", captcha);
            ViewData["CaptchaCode"] = captcha;
        }

        public async Task OnGetAsync(string? returnUrl = null)
        {
            await HttpContext.SignOutAsync(CookieAuthenticationDefaults.AuthenticationScheme);
            HttpContext.Session.Remove("JwtToken");
            HttpContext.Session.Remove("AvatarUrl");

            ReturnUrl = returnUrl ?? Url.Content("~/Employee/TongQuanView");

            GenerateCaptcha();
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostAsync(string? returnUrl = null)
        {
            if (!ModelState.IsValid)
            {
                GenerateCaptcha(); 
                return Page();
            }

            var expectedCaptcha = HttpContext.Session.GetString("CaptchaCode");
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(expectedCaptcha) || !string.Equals(expectedCaptcha, Input.CaptchaResult, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                ModelState.AddModelError("Input.CaptchaResult", "Mã xác thực không chính xác.");
                GenerateCaptcha(); 
                return Page();
            }

            try
            {
                var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
                var apiRequest = new LoginRequest
                {
                    Username = Input.TenDangNhap,
                    Password = Input.MatKhau
                };

                var response = await httpClient.PostAsJsonAsync("api/shared/Auth/login-nhan-vien", apiRequest);

                if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                {
                    var apiResponse = await response.Content.ReadFromJsonAsync<LoginResponse>();

                    if (apiResponse != null && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(apiResponse.Token))
                    {
                        var claims = new List<Claim>
                        {
                            new Claim(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier, apiResponse.IdNhanVien.ToString()),
                            new Claim(ClaimTypes.Name, apiResponse.HoTen),
                            new Claim(ClaimTypes.Role, apiResponse.TenVaiTro)
                        };

                        if (apiResponse.Quyen != null)
                        {
                            foreach (var quyen in apiResponse.Quyen)
                            {
                                claims.Add(new Claim("Permission", quyen));
                            }
                        }

                        var claimsIdentity = new ClaimsIdentity(claims, CookieAuthenticationDefaults.AuthenticationScheme);
                        var authProperties = new AuthenticationProperties
                        {
                            ExpiresUtc = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow.AddHours(8),
                            IsPersistent = true
                        };

                        await HttpContext.SignInAsync(CookieAuthenticationDefaults.AuthenticationScheme, new ClaimsPrincipal(claimsIdentity), authProperties);

                        string avatar = apiResponse.AnhDaiDien ?? "";
                        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(avatar) && !avatar.StartsWith("http"))
                        {
                            var apiBaseUrl = httpClient.BaseAddress?.ToString().TrimEnd('/');
                            if (!avatar.StartsWith("/")) avatar = "/" + avatar;
                            avatar = $"{apiBaseUrl}{avatar}";
                        }

                        HttpContext.Session.SetString("JwtToken", apiResponse.Token);
                        HttpContext.Session.SetString("AvatarUrl", avatar);

                        HttpContext.Session.Remove("CaptchaCode");

                        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(returnUrl) || returnUrl == "/")
                        {
                            return RedirectToPage("/Employee/TongQuanView");
                        }

                        return LocalRedirect(returnUrl);
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    var errorContent = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                    try
                    {
                        var errorJson = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonElement>(errorContent);
                        if (errorJson.TryGetProperty("message", out var msg))
                        {
                            ErrorMessage = msg.GetString();
                            GenerateCaptcha(); 
                            return Page();
                        }
                    }
                    catch { }
                }

                ErrorMessage = "Tài khoản hoặc mật khẩu không chính xác.";
                GenerateCaptcha();
                return Page();
            }
            catch (Exception)
            {
                ErrorMessage = "Không thể kết nối đến máy chủ. Vui lòng thử lại sau.";
                GenerateCaptcha();
                return Page();
            }
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostLogout()
        {
            HttpContext.Session.Clear();
            await HttpContext.SignOutAsync(CookieAuthenticationDefaults.AuthenticationScheme);
            return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee");
        }
    }
}

        <div class="col-lg-7 col-xl-8">

                <div class="card-header bg-white p-4 border-0 d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                    <div class="d-flex align-items-center gap-2">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined text-success">history_edu</span>
                        <h5 class="mb-0 fw-bold text-dark">Lịch Sử Đơn Của Bạn</h5>
                    </div>
                    <button class="btn btn-icon material-ripple" id="btnRefresh" title="Làm mới">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined">refresh</span>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div class="card-body p-4 pt-0">
                    <div id="history-container" class="dxn-history-scroll">
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";

        // Thiết lập giá trị min cho input date là ngày hôm nay
        const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
        document.getElementById("txtTuNgay").setAttribute("min", today);
        document.getElementById("txtDenNgay").setAttribute("min", today);

        // Ràng buộc Từ ngày <= Đến ngày
        $("#txtTuNgay").on("change", function() {
            $("#txtDenNgay").setAttribute("min", this.value);
        });

        // Load Lịch sử
        async function loadHistory() {
            $("#history-container").html('<div class="text-center p-4"><div class="spinner-border text-primary"></div></div>');
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/history`, {
                    headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` }
                });
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Lỗi tải dữ liệu");
                const data = await res.json();
                renderHistory(data);
            } catch (err) {
                $("#history-container").html(`<div class="alert alert-danger m-3">${err.message}</div>`);
            }
        }

        function renderHistory(list) {
            const $cont = $("#history-container").empty();
            if (list.length === 0) {
                $cont.html('<div class="text-center text-muted p-5"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 text-light">inbox</span><br/>Bạn chưa có đơn xin nghỉ nào.</div>');
                return;
            }

            list.forEach(item => {
                let badgeClass = "bg-warning text-dark"; // Chờ duyệt
                if (item.trangThai === "Đã duyệt") badgeClass = "bg-success text-white";
                if (item.trangThai === "Đã từ chối") badgeClass = "bg-danger text-white";

                const formatDate = (dateStr) => {
                    const d = new Date(dateStr);
                    return d.toLocaleDateString('vi-VN');
                };

                const ghiChuHtml = item.ghiChuPheDuyet
                    ? `<div class="mt-2 pt-2 border-top small"><span class="fw-bold text-dark">Phản hồi từ ${item.nguoiDuyet}:</span> <span class="text-primary fst-italic">${item.ghiChuPheDuyet}</span></div>`
                    : '';

                $cont.append(`
                    <div class="dxn-history-item mb-3">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-start mb-2">
                            <h6 class="fw-bold m-0" style="color: #4E342E;">${item.loaiDon}</h6>
                            <span class="badge ${badgeClass} rounded-pill px-3 py-1">${item.trangThai}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-muted small mb-2 d-flex align-items-center">
                            <span class="material-symbols-outlined me-1" style="font-size: 16px;">calendar_month</span>
                            ${formatDate(item.ngayBatDau)} &rarr; ${formatDate(item.ngayKetThuc)}
                        </div>
                        <div class="small" style="color: #616161;">
                            <span class="fw-bold">Lý do:</span> ${item.lyDo}
                        </div>
                        ${ghiChuHtml}
                    </div>
                `);
            });
        }

        // Submit Đơn
        $("#formTaoDon").submit(async function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            const tuNgay = $("#txtTuNgay").val();
            const denNgay = $("#txtDenNgay").val();

            if(tuNgay > denNgay) {
                Swal.fire("Lỗi", "Ngày kết thúc phải lớn hơn hoặc bằng ngày bắt đầu.", "error");
                return;
            }

            const payload = {
                loaiDon: $("#cboLoaiDon").val(),
                lyDo: $("#txtLyDo").val().trim(),
                ngayBatDau: tuNgay,
                ngayKetThuc: denNgay
            };

            const btn = $("#btnSubmitDon");
            btn.prop("disabled", true).html('<div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2"></div> Đang gửi...');

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/create`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
                });
                
                const data = await res.json();
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.message || "Đã xảy ra lỗi");

                Swal.fire("Thành công", data.message, "success");
                $("#formTaoDon")[0].reset();
                loadHistory();
            } catch (err) {
                Swal.fire("Lỗi Gửi Đơn", err.message, "error");
            } finally {
                btn.prop("disabled", false).html('<span class="material-symbols-outlined me-2">send</span> Gửi Đơn Xin Nghỉ');
            }
        });

        $(document).ready(() => {
            loadHistory();
            $("#btnRefresh").click(loadHistory);
        });
    </script>
}

================================================================================
FILE: E:/Tai Lieu Hoc Tap/N19 KLTN 032026/Cafebook/WebCafebookApi/Pages\Employee\DonXinNghiView.cshtml.cs
================================================================================
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class DonXinNghiViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;

        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public DonXinNghiViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet()
        {
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken))
            {
                string currentUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString;
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = currentUrl });
            }

            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/donxinnghiweb";

            return Page();
        }
    }
}

                    <button type="button" class="btn btn-outline-danger w-100 fw-bold rounded-pill py-2" id="btnBoChonKhuyenMai">Bỏ chọn Khuyến mãi</button>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _idHoaDon = parseInt('@Model.IdHoaDon');
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";
        const _defaultImage = "@HinhAnhPaths.WebDefaultFoodIcon";

        let _allSanPhams = [];
        let _chiTietItems = {};
        let _currentPromoId = 0;
        let _currentPromoName = "";
        let _currentDiscount = 0; // Biến mới: Lưu trữ mức giảm giá hiện tại đề phòng API trả về thiếu
        
        // Cập nhật hàm formatCurrency để chống lỗi hiển thị NaN nếu giá trị bị null/undefined
        const formatCurrency = (number) => new Intl.NumberFormat('vi-VN', { style: 'currency', currency: 'VND' }).format(number || 0);

        async function callApi(endpoint, method, data) {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/${endpoint}`, {
                    method: method, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    body: data ? JSON.stringify(data) : null
                });
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(await res.text());
                const contentType = res.headers.get("content-type");
                return contentType && contentType.includes("json") ? await res.json() : await res.text();
            } catch (err) {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi Thao Tác', err.message, 'error');
                return null;
            }
        }

        async function loadData() {
            const data = await callApi(`load/${_idHoaDon}`, 'GET');
            if(data) {
                _allSanPhams = data.sanPhams;
                data.chiTietItems.forEach(item => _chiTietItems[item.idChiTietHoaDon] = item);
                
                // Render Categories
                data.danhMucs.forEach(dm => $("#category-list").append(`<li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link" href="#" data-id="${dm.idDanhMuc}"><span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle fs-6">label</span> ${dm.tenLoaiSP}</a></li>`));
                
                // Render Promos
                data.khuyenMais.forEach(km => $("#cboKhuyenMai").append(`<option value="${km.idKhuyenMai}">${km.tenKhuyenMai}</option>`));
                
                renderProducts(_allSanPhams);
                renderBill(data.hoaDonInfo);
            }
        }

        function renderProducts(list) {
            const $list = $("#product-list").empty();
            if(!list.length) return $list.html('<p class="text-center text-muted p-4 w-100"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1">fastfood</span><br/>Không có sản phẩm</p>');
            
            list.forEach((sp, index) => {
                const delay = (index % 10) * 0.05; // Hiệu ứng xuất hiện mượt mà
                $list.append(`
                    <div class="gmw-product-card anim-item shadow-sm" style="animation-delay: ${delay}s" data-id="${sp.idSanPham}">
                        <img src="${sp.hinhAnh}" onerror="this.onerror=null; this.src='${_defaultImage}';">
                        <div class="p-2 text-center">
                            <div class="gmw-product-name text-truncate fw-bold">${sp.tenSanPham}</div>
                            <div class="gmw-product-price text-danger fw-bold">${formatCurrency(sp.donGia)}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `);
                $list.children().last().data('sanpham', sp);
            });
        }

        // [NÂNG CẤP]: Hàm renderBill tự động tính toán lại toàn bộ tiền
        function renderBill(info) {
            // Đồng nhất object dữ liệu: Bắt cả trường hợp API trả về info.updatedHoaDonInfo
            let billData = (info && info.updatedHoaDonInfo) ? info.updatedHoaDonInfo : (info || {});

            const $body = $("#bill-details-body").empty();
            const items = Object.values(_chiTietItems).sort((a, b) => a.idChiTietHoaDon - b.idChiTietHoaDon);
    
            // 1. TỰ TÍNH TIỀN GỐC TỪ GIỎ HÀNG THỰC TẾ TRÊN MÀN HÌNH
            let localTongTienGoc = 0;

            if(!items.length) {
                $body.html('<tr><td colspan="3" class="text-center text-muted py-5 fst-italic">Chưa có món nào trong đơn.</td></tr>');
            } else {
                items.forEach(item => {
                    const lineTotal = item.donGia * item.soLuong;
                    localTongTienGoc += lineTotal;

                    $body.append(`
                        <tr class="anim-item">
                            <td>
                                <div class="fw-bold text-dark">${item.tenSanPham}</div>
                                <div class="text-muted small">
                                    ${formatCurrency(item.donGia)} x ${item.soLuong} = <span class="text-danger fw-bold">${formatCurrency(lineTotal)}</span>
                                </div>
                                ${item.ghiChu ? `<div class="small mt-1"><span class="badge bg-warning text-dark"><span class="material-symbols-outlined" style="font-size: 11px;">edit_note</span> ${item.ghiChu}</span></div>` : ''}
                            </td>
                            <td>
                                <div class="d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center gap-1 qty-control shadow-sm border rounded-pill overflow-hidden bg-white">
                                    <button class="btn btn-sm px-2 py-0 fs-5 btn-giam text-dark" data-id="${item.idChiTietHoaDon}">-</button>
                                    <input type="text" class="form-control text-center px-1 fw-bold input-qty border-0"
                                           value="${item.soLuong}" data-id="${item.idChiTietHoaDon}"
                                           style="width: 35px; height: 30px; font-size: 14px; box-shadow: none;">
                                    <button class="btn btn-sm px-2 py-0 fs-5 btn-tang text-dark" data-id="${item.idChiTietHoaDon}">+</button>
                                </div>
                            </td>
                            <td class="text-center">
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-light text-danger btn-xoa rounded-circle p-2 shadow-sm" data-id="${item.idChiTietHoaDon}">
                                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-5 d-block">delete</span>
                                </button>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    `);
                });
            }

            // 2. Cập nhật mức giảm giá (Nếu API có trả về thì lấy, không thì giữ mức cũ)
            if (billData.giamGia !== undefined) {
                _currentDiscount = billData.giamGia;
            }

            // 3. Tính Thành Tiền Cuối Cùng
            let thanhTien = localTongTienGoc - _currentDiscount;
            if (thanhTien < 0) thanhTien = 0;

            // 4. Đẩy số liệu lên Giao diện
            if (billData.soBan) $("#lblTieuDeHoaDon").text(`Hóa đơn - Bàn ${billData.soBan}`);
            $("#lblTongTien").text(formatCurrency(localTongTienGoc));
            $("#lblTienGiam").text(formatCurrency(_currentDiscount));
            $("#lblThanhTien").text(formatCurrency(thanhTien));
    
            // 5. Cập nhật trạng thái Khuyến Mãi
            _currentPromoId = billData.idKhuyenMai || _currentPromoId || 0;
            if(_currentPromoId === 0) {
                $("#lblTenKhuyenMaiDangDung").text("");
                $("#btnMoPopupKhuyenMai").text("Chọn Mã").removeClass("btn-success").addClass("btn-outline-primary");
            }
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
            // FIX LỖI POPUP KHUYẾN MÃI BỊ CHE KHUẤT BỞI NAVBAR
            $("#modalKhuyenMai").appendTo("body");

            loadData();

            // Filter UI
            $("#category-list").on("click", ".nav-link", function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $("#category-list .nav-link").removeClass("active"); $(this).addClass("active");
                const catId = $(this).data("id");
                const kw = $("#search-bar").val().toLowerCase();
                let filtered = catId ? _allSanPhams.filter(s => s.idDanhMuc == catId) : _allSanPhams;
                if(kw) filtered = filtered.filter(s => s.tenSanPham.toLowerCase().includes(kw));
                renderProducts(filtered);
            });

            $("#search-bar").on("keyup", () => $("#category-list .active").click());

            // Add Product
            $("#product-list").on("click", ".gmw-product-card", async function() {
                const sp = $(this).data('sanpham');
                const { value: note } = await Swal.fire({ title: `Thêm ${sp.tenSanPham}`, input: 'text', inputPlaceholder: 'Ghi chú (không bắt buộc)', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#6F4E37', cancelButtonColor: '#9E9E9E', confirmButtonText: 'Thêm', cancelButtonText: 'Hủy' });
                if(note !== undefined) {
                    const res = await callApi('add-item', 'POST', { idHoaDon: _idHoaDon, idSanPham: sp.idSanPham, soLuong: 1, ghiChu: note.trim() });
                    if(res) { _chiTietItems[res.newItem.idChiTietHoaDon] = res.newItem; renderBill(res.updatedHoaDonInfo); }
                }
            });

            // ==========================================
            // XỬ LÝ SỐ LƯỢNG MỚI (CHỐNG LAG & TÍNH TOÁN LẠI)
            // ==========================================
            const changeQty = async (id, delta) => {
                const item = _chiTietItems[id];
                const res = await callApi('update-quantity', 'PUT', { idChiTietHoaDon: id, soLuongMoi: item.soLuong + delta });
                if(res) {
                    if(item.soLuong + delta <= 0) delete _chiTietItems[id];
                    else item.soLuong += delta;
                    renderBill(res);
                }
            };
            
            $("#bill-details-body").on("click", ".btn-tang", function() { changeQty($(this).data("id"), 1); });
            $("#bill-details-body").on("click", ".btn-giam", function() { changeQty($(this).data("id"), -1); });

            // Khi người dùng gõ số và click ra ngoài (Blur)
            $("#bill-details-body").on("blur", ".input-qty", async function() {
                const id = $(this).data("id");
                const item = _chiTietItems[id];
                let newQty = parseInt($(this).val());

                if (isNaN(newQty) || newQty < 0) {
                    $(this).val(item.soLuong); // Khôi phục lại số cũ nếu nhập bậy bạ
                    return;
                }

                if (newQty !== item.soLuong) {
                    const res = await callApi('update-quantity', 'PUT', { idChiTietHoaDon: id, soLuongMoi: newQty });
                    if(res) {
                        if(newQty <= 0) delete _chiTietItems[id];
                        else item.soLuong = newQty;
                        renderBill(res);
                    } else {
                        $(this).val(item.soLuong); // Khôi phục nếu API báo lỗi (vd kho hết)
                    }
                }
            });

            // Khi người dùng đang nhập và bấm Enter
            $("#bill-details-body").on("keydown", ".input-qty", function(e) {
                if (e.key === "Enter") {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    $(this).blur(); // Ép kích hoạt sự kiện blur ở trên
                }
            });
            
            // Delete Item
            $("#bill-details-body").on("click", ".btn-xoa", async function() {
                const id = $(this).data("id");
                if((await Swal.fire({title:'Xóa món?', icon:'warning', showCancelButton:true, confirmButtonColor:'#D32F2F', cancelButtonText: 'Không'})).isConfirmed){
                    const res = await callApi(`delete-item/${id}`, 'DELETE');
                    if(res) { delete _chiTietItems[id]; renderBill(res); }
                }
            });

            // ==========================================
            // XỬ LÝ CÁC NÚT THAO TÁC MỚI
            // ==========================================
            
            // Send to Kitchen
            $("#btnGuiBep").click(async function() {
                const res = await callApi(`send-to-kitchen/${_idHoaDon}`, 'POST');
                if(res) Swal.fire({title: 'Thành công', text: 'Đã báo bếp thành công!', icon: 'success', confirmButtonColor: '#6F4E37'});
            });

            // In Phiếu
            $("#btnInPhieu").click(async function() {
                const res = await callApi(`print-and-notify-kitchen/${_idHoaDon}`, 'POST');
                if(res) {
                    Swal.fire({ title: 'Thành công', text: 'Đã gửi lệnh in phiếu và báo bếp!', icon: 'success', timer: 2000, showConfirmButton: false });
                }
            });

            // Hủy Đơn
            $("#btnHuyDon").click(async function() {
                const confirm = await Swal.fire({
                    title: 'Xác nhận Hủy?',
                    text: 'Bạn có chắc chắn muốn hủy hóa đơn này không? Toàn bộ món sẽ bị xóa.',
                    icon: 'error',
                    showCancelButton: true,
                    confirmButtonColor: '#D32F2F',
                    cancelButtonColor: '#9E9E9E',
                    confirmButtonText: 'Đồng ý Hủy'
                });

                if(confirm.isConfirmed) {
                    const res = await callApi(`cancel-order/${_idHoaDon}`, 'PUT');
                    if(res) {
                        window.location.href = '/nhan-vien/so-do-ban';
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        // Xử lý Popup Khuyến Mãi
        $('#modalKhuyenMai').on('show.bs.modal', async function () {
            const $container = $("#promo-list-container");
            $container.html('<div class="text-center p-4"><div class="spinner-border text-primary-coffee"></div><p class="mt-3 text-muted fw-bold">Đang tải mã...</p></div>');
    
            const promos = await callApi(`khuyenmai-available/${_idHoaDon}`, 'GET');
            if(promos) {
                $container.empty();
                if(promos.length === 0) {
                    $container.html('<div class="text-center text-muted p-4"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 mb-2">sentiment_dissatisfied</span><br/>Không có mã khuyến mãi nào phù hợp.</div>');
                    return;
                }

                promos.forEach(km => {
                    const isDis = km.isEligible ? "" : "disabled opacity-50";
                    const reasonHtml = km.isEligible ? `<div class="fs-6 fw-bold text-success mt-2">- ${formatCurrency(km.calculatedDiscount)}</div>` : `<div class="text-danger small mt-2 fw-bold"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">error</span> ${km.ineligibilityReason}</div>`;
                    const activeBadge = (_currentPromoId === km.idKhuyenMai) ? '<span class="badge bg-success position-absolute top-0 end-0 m-3 shadow-sm">Đang Dùng</span>' : '';

                    $container.append(`
                        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm mb-3 position-relative ${isDis}" style="border-radius: 16px; cursor: pointer;" data-id="${km.idKhuyenMai}" data-eligible="${km.isEligible}" data-name="${km.tenChuongTrinh}">
                            ${activeBadge}
                            <div class="card-body p-3 d-flex gap-3 align-items-center">
                                <div class="bg-primary-subtle text-primary-coffee rounded-circle p-3 d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center">
                                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-3">local_activity</span>
                                </div>
                                <div>
                                    <h6 class="fw-bold mb-1 text-dark">${km.maKhuyenMai} - ${km.tenChuongTrinh}</h6>
                                    <div class="small text-muted">${km.dieuKienApDung}</div>
                                    ${reasonHtml}
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `);
                });
            }
        });

        // Click chọn 1 Khuyến Mãi trong Popup
        $("#promo-list-container").on("click", ".card", async function() {
            if($(this).data("eligible") === false) return; // Bỏ qua nếu ko đủ điều kiện

            const idKM = $(this).data("id");
            _currentPromoName = $(this).data("name");

            const res = await callApi('apply-promotion', 'PUT', { idHoaDon: _idHoaDon, idKhuyenMai: idKM });
            if(res) {
                $('#modalKhuyenMai').modal('hide');
                $("#lblTenKhuyenMaiDangDung").text(`Áp dụng: ${_currentPromoName}`);
                $("#btnMoPopupKhuyenMai").text("Đổi Mã").removeClass("btn-outline-primary").addClass("btn-success");
                renderBill(res);
                Swal.fire({ title: 'Áp mã thành công!', icon: 'success', toast: true, position: 'top-end', showConfirmButton: false, timer: 2000 });
            }
        });

        // Nút Bỏ chọn Khuyến mãi
        $("#btnBoChonKhuyenMai").click(async function() {
            if(_currentPromoId === 0) return $('#modalKhuyenMai').modal('hide');

            const res = await callApi('apply-promotion', 'PUT', { idHoaDon: _idHoaDon, idKhuyenMai: 0 });
            if(res) {
                $('#modalKhuyenMai').modal('hide');
                _currentPromoName = "";
                renderBill(res);
                Swal.fire({ title: 'Đã hủy mã giảm giá!', icon: 'info', toast: true, position: 'top-end', showConfirmButton: false, timer: 2000 });
            }
        });
    </script>
}

================================================================================
FILE: E:/Tai Lieu Hoc Tap/N19 KLTN 032026/Cafebook/WebCafebookApi/Pages\Employee\GoiMonView.cshtml.cs
================================================================================
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.DataProtection;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class GoiMonViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        private readonly IDataProtector _protector;

        public int IdHoaDon { get; set; }
        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        [TempData]
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; set; }

        public GoiMonViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory, IDataProtectionProvider provider)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
            _protector = provider.CreateProtector("Cafebook.HoaDon.Security");
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet(string? maHoaDon)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(maHoaDon))
            {
                TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Không tìm thấy thông tin Hóa đơn.";
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/SoDoBanView");
            }

            try
            {
                string rawId = _protector.Unprotect(maHoaDon);
                IdHoaDon = int.Parse(rawId);
            }
            catch (Exception)
            {
                ErrorMessage = "Mã đường dẫn không hợp lệ hoặc đã bị can thiệp!";
                return Page();
            }

            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken))
            {
                string currentUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString;
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = currentUrl });
            }

            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/goimonweb";

            return Page();
        }
    }
}

FILE: E:/Tai Lieu Hoc Tap/N19 KLTN 032026/Cafebook/WebCafebookApi/Pages\Employee\HoTroKhachHangView.cshtml

﻿@page "/nhan-vien/ho-tro-khach-hang/"
@model WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee.HoTroKhachHangViewModel
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Trung tâm Hỗ trợ Khách hàng";

@section Styles {
    <link href="~/css/HoTroKhachHang.css" rel="stylesheet" asp-append-version="true" />
}

<div class="htnv-dashboard-grid" id="mainDashboard">
<div class="htnv-ticket-list-wrapper">
    <div class="htnv-header-box">
        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-2">
                <h5 class="m-0"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-4">support_agent</span> Hộp thư hỗ trợ</h5>

            <div class="form-check form-switch small">

    <div class="htnv-chat-column" id="chat-column">

                <div class="htnv-chat-info">
                    <strong id="chatHeaderName" class="mb-1 text-dark"></strong>
                    <span class="badge bg-success-subtle text-success border border-success-subtle rounded-pill" id="chatHeaderStatus"></span>

        <div class="htnv-chat-history" id="chat-history">

                <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 mb-2">forum</span>
                <p>Vui lòng chọn một phiếu hỗ trợ từ danh sách bên trái.</p>
            </div>

        <form method="post" id="chatForm" class="htnv-chat-form" asp-antiforgery="true">
            <input type="hidden" id="JwtToken" value="@Model.JwtToken" />
            <input id="chatMessageInput" class="htnv-chat-input" placeholder="Nhập tin nhắn phản hồi khách hàng..." autocomplete="off" disabled />
            
            <button type="submit" id="sendButton" class="htnv-btn-send shadow-sm" disabled>
                <span class="material-symbols-outlined">send</span>
            </button>
            <button type="button" id="resolveButton" class="btn btn-outline-success fw-bold rounded-pill px-4 ms-2 shadow-sm d-none d-md-block" disabled>
                Đánh dấu Đã xử lý
            </button>
        </form>
    </div>

    <div class="htnv-summary-col" id="summary-column">
        <div class="htnv-summary-header shadow-sm">
            <div class="d-flex align-items-center gap-2">
                <button class="btn-icon-circular text-white d-lg-none me-1" id="btnBackToChat" style="background: rgba(255,255,255,0.2);"><span class="material-symbols-outlined">arrow_back</span></button>
                <span>Thông Tin Phiếu</span>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="htnv-summary-body" id="summary-card-content">
            <div class="h-100 d-flex flex-column align-items-center justify-content-center text-muted opacity-50">
                <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 mb-2">assignment</span>
                <p>Chưa chọn phiếu.</p>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
