@section Scripts {
    <partial name="_ValidationScriptsPartial" />
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/microsoft-signalr/8.0.0/signalr.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        const apiBaseUrl = '@Model.ApiBaseUrl'.replace(/\/$/, "");

        $(document).ready(function () {
        const $ticketListContainer = $('#ticket-list-container');
        const $chatHistory = $('#chat-history');
        const $chatInput = $('#chatMessageInput');
        const $sendButton = $('#sendButton');
        const $resolveButton = $('#resolveButton');
        const $chatForm = $('#chatForm');
                        
        const jwtToken = $('#JwtToken').val() || null;
        const antiForgeryToken = $('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]').val();

        const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'RequestVerificationToken': antiForgeryToken };
        if (jwtToken) headers['Authorization'] = 'Bearer ' + jwtToken;

        // Biến quản lý trạng thái Chat hiện tại
        let currentTicketId = null;
        let currentGroupName = null;
        let currentTicketData = null;
                
        // Biến dùng cho tính năng cuộn tải tin nhắn cũ
        let _allChatMessages = [];
        let _displayedIndex = 0;
        const PAGE_SIZE = 8;

        // Biến dùng cho tính năng Lazy Load danh sách phiếu
        let currentSkip = 0;
        const TAKE_COUNT = 5;
        let isFetchingTickets = false;
        let hasMoreTickets = true;
        let searchTimeout = null;

        /* =========================================================
        1. CẤU HÌNH SIGNALR
        ========================================================= */
        const hubOptions = jwtToken ? { accessTokenFactory: () => jwtToken } : {};
        const hubConnection = new signalR.HubConnectionBuilder()
        .withUrl(apiBaseUrl + "/chatHub", hubOptions)
        .build();
                        
        hubConnection.on("ReceiveMessage", function (message) {
        const idTicket = message.idThongBaoHoTro || message.IdThongBaoHoTro;
        // Nếu tin nhắn thuộc về người đang chat, hiển thị luôn
        if (currentTicketId && idTicket == currentTicketId) {
        _allChatMessages.push(message);
        _displayedIndex++;
        appendSingleMessage(message, true);
        } else {
        // Cập nhật lại danh sách bên trái để báo hiệu có tin mới (Load lại từ đầu)
        loadTicketList(false);
        }
        });
                    
        // Khi có thay đổi trạng thái (tạo phiếu mới, đóng phiếu), tải lại danh sách
        hubConnection.on("ReloadTicketList", () => loadTicketList(false));
                    
        async function startConnection() {
        try { await hubConnection.start(); } catch (err) { console.error("SignalR Error", err); }
        }

        /* =========================================================
        2. HÀM VẼ GIAO DIỆN TIN NHẮN
        ========================================================= */
        function generateMessageHtml(msg) {
        const isUser = msg.loaiTinNhan === 'KhachHang';
        const isStaff = msg.loaiTinNhan === 'NhanVien';
        const rowClass = isUser ? 'htnv-user-row' : (isStaff ? 'htnv-staff-row' : 'htnv-bot-row');
        const avatarIcon = isUser ? 'person' : (isStaff ? 'support_agent' : 'smart_toy');
                        
        // Tiền xử lý text (xuống dòng, in đậm, xóa button)
        let cleanText = (msg.noiDung || '').replace(/\[BUTTON:\s*(.*?)\s*\|\s*(.*?)\]/g, "");
        cleanText = cleanText.replace(/\n/g, '<br />').replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
        const time = new Date(msg.thoiGian).toLocaleTimeString('vi-VN', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
                        
        return `
        <div class="htnv-message-row ${rowClass}">
        <div class="htnv-avatar ${isUser ? 'htnv-avatar-user' : (isStaff ? 'htnv-avatar-staff' : 'htnv-avatar-bot')} shadow-sm">
        <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-5">${avatarIcon}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="htnv-msg-content">
        <div class="htnv-bubble ${isUser ? 'htnv-bubble-user' : (isStaff ? 'htnv-bubble-staff' : 'htnv-bubble-bot')}">${cleanText}</div>
        <div class="htnv-bubble-time ${isUser ? 'text-end' : 'text-start'}">${time}</div>
        </div>
        </div>`;
        }

        function prependSingleMessage(msg) {
        $chatHistory.prepend(generateMessageHtml(msg));
        }

        function appendSingleMessage(msg, scroll = true) {
        $chatHistory.append(generateMessageHtml(msg));
        if(scroll) $chatHistory.scrollTop($chatHistory[0].scrollHeight);
        }

        function loadMoreMessages() {
        if (_displayedIndex >= _allChatMessages.length) return;
        const prevHeight = $chatHistory[0].scrollHeight;
                        
        const nextBatch = _allChatMessages.slice(
        Math.max(0, _allChatMessages.length - _displayedIndex - PAGE_SIZE),
        _allChatMessages.length - _displayedIndex
        );
                        
        nextBatch.reverse().forEach(msg => prependSingleMessage(msg));
        _displayedIndex += nextBatch.length;
        $chatHistory.scrollTop($chatHistory[0].scrollHeight - prevHeight);
        }

        /* =========================================================
        3. LOAD DỮ LIỆU TICKET (LAZY LOAD & SEARCH SERVER-SIDE)
        ========================================================= */
        async function loadTicketList(isAppend = false) {
        // Chặn gọi API nếu đang tải hoặc nếu kéo xuống mà đã hết dữ liệu
        if (isFetchingTickets || (!hasMoreTickets && isAppend)) return;
        isFetchingTickets = true;

        try {
        const isOnlyPending = $('#chkOnlyPending').is(':checked');
        const searchTerm = $('#ticketSearchInput').val().trim();
                    
        if (!isAppend) {
        // Reset lại trạng thái phân trang nếu tải mới từ đầu
        currentSkip = 0;
        hasMoreTickets = true;
        $ticketListContainer.empty();
        $ticketListContainer.html('<div class="p-5 text-center text-muted"><div class="spinner-border text-primary-coffee mb-3"></div><p>Đang tải...</p></div>');
        } else {
        // Thêm UI loading xoay vòng ở cuối danh sách khi cuộn
        $ticketListContainer.append('<div id="ticket-loading-more" class="text-center py-2"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm text-primary-coffee"></div></div>');
        }

        // Gọi API với phân trang
        const url = `${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/nhanvien/hotro/tickets?skip=${currentSkip}&take=${TAKE_COUNT}&onlyPending=${isOnlyPending}&search=${encodeURIComponent(searchTerm)}`;
        const response = await fetch(url, { method: 'GET', headers: headers });
        const tickets = await response.json();
                    
        if (!isAppend) $ticketListContainer.empty();
        $('#ticket-loading-more').remove();

        if (tickets.length === 0) {
        hasMoreTickets = false;
        if (!isAppend) {
        $ticketListContainer.html('<div class="p-5 text-center text-muted opacity-75">Không có yêu cầu nào.</div>');
        }
        return;
        }

        // Nếu số lượng trả về ít hơn TAKE_COUNT nghĩa là đã chạm đáy DB
        if (tickets.length < TAKE_COUNT) hasMoreTickets = false;

        tickets.forEach(ticket => {
        const isPending = ticket.trangThai === 'Chờ xử lý';
        $ticketListContainer.append(`
        <div class="htnv-ticket-item ${isPending ? 'htnv-status-pending' : ''} ${ticket.idThongBao == currentTicketId ? 'active' : ''}" data-id="${ticket.idThongBao}">
        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-1">
        <strong class="text-truncate">${ticket.tenKhachHang}</strong>
        <span class="htnv-ticket-time fw-medium ${isPending ? 'text-accent' : 'text-success'}">${ticket.trangThai}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="htnv-ticket-preview">${ticket.noiDungYeuCau || '...'}</div>
        ${isPending ? '<span class="htnv-status-indicator"></span>' : ''}
        </div>`);
        });

        currentSkip += tickets.length;
        } catch (e) {
        console.error("Lỗi tải danh sách", e);
        $('#ticket-loading-more').remove();
        } finally {
        isFetchingTickets = false;
        }
        }

        async function loadTicketDetail(id) {
        currentTicketId = id;
        $('#mainDashboard').addClass('show-chat');
        $('.htnv-ticket-item').removeClass('active');
        $(`.htnv-ticket-item[data-id="${id}"]`).addClass('active');

        $chatInput.prop('disabled', true);
        $sendButton.prop('disabled', true);
        $chatHistory.html('<div class="h-100 d-flex justify-content-center align-items-center"><div class="spinner-border text-primary-coffee"></div></div>');
                                
        try {
        const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/nhanvien/hotro/ticket/${id}`, { method: 'GET', headers: headers });
        const ticketData = await response.json();
        currentTicketData = ticketData;
                        
        $chatHistory.empty();
        _allChatMessages = ticketData.lichSuChat || [];
        _displayedIndex = 0;

        if (_allChatMessages.length > 0) {
        loadMoreMessages();
        $chatHistory.scrollTop($chatHistory[0].scrollHeight);
        } else {
        $chatHistory.html('<div class="h-100 d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center text-muted">Chưa có tin nhắn</div>');
        }

        // Cập nhật Cột thông tin bên phải (Summary)
        $('#summary-card-content').html(`
        <div class="htnv-request-content mb-3 shadow-sm">
        <span class="badge bg-light text-dark border mb-2">#${ticketData.idThongBao}</span>
        <div class="fw-bold mb-1">Yêu cầu ban đầu:</div>
        <div class="text-muted small">${ticketData.noiDungYeuCau || 'Không có mô tả'}</div>
        </div>
        ${ticketData.ghiChuTuAI ? `
        <div class="htnv-request-content shadow-sm" style="border-left: 4px solid var(--cf-accent);">
        <div class="fw-bold mb-1 text-accent">Ghi chú hệ thống:</div>
        <div class="text-muted small">${ticketData.ghiChuTuAI}</div>
        </div>` : ''}
        `);

        $('#chat-header').css('visibility', 'visible');
        $('#chatHeaderName').text(ticketData.tenKhachHang);
        $('#chatHeaderStatus').text(ticketData.trangThai);

        // THIẾT LẬP JOIN PHÒNG SIGNALR
        const newGroupName = (ticketData.idKhachHang && ticketData.idKhachHang > 0)
        ? `khach_${ticketData.idKhachHang}`
        : `guest_${ticketData.guestSessionId}`;
                                                
        if (currentGroupName !== newGroupName) {
        currentGroupName = newGroupName;
        if (hubConnection.state === signalR.HubConnectionState.Connected) {
        await hubConnection.invoke("JoinGroup", currentGroupName);
        }
        }

        // Mở khóa input
        if (ticketData.trangThai !== 'Đã xử lý') {
        $chatInput.prop('disabled', false);
        $sendButton.prop('disabled', false);
        $resolveButton.prop('disabled', false);
        } else {
        $resolveButton.prop('disabled', true);
        }
        } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
        }

        /* =========================================================
        4. CÁC SỰ KIỆN TƯƠNG TÁC
        ========================================================= */
        // Tải thêm tin nhắn cũ khi cuộn đoạn Chat lên trên cùng
        $chatHistory.on('scroll', function() {
        if ($(this).scrollTop() === 0 && _displayedIndex < _allChatMessages.length) {
        loadMoreMessages();
        }
        });

        // Tải thêm phiếu khi cuộn Danh sách phiếu xuống dưới cùng
        $ticketListContainer.on('scroll', function() {
        // Cộng thêm sai số khoảng 10px để bắt event nhạy hơn
        if ($(this).scrollTop() + $(this).innerHeight() >= $(this)[0].scrollHeight - 10) {
        loadTicketList(true);
        }
        });

        // Thay đổi bộ lọc Trạng thái -> Load lại từ đầu
        $('#chkOnlyPending').on('change', () => loadTicketList(false));
                
        // Gõ vào thanh tìm kiếm -> Đợi 500ms mới gọi API (Debounce)
        $('#ticketSearchInput').on('keyup', function () {
        clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
        searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => loadTicketList(false), 500);
        });

        $ticketListContainer.on('click', '.htnv-ticket-item', function () {
        loadTicketDetail($(this).data('id'));
        });

        // GỬI TIN NHẮN (SIGNALR)
        $chatForm.on('submit', async function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (!currentTicketId || !currentGroupName || !currentTicketData) return;
                                
        const text = $chatInput.val().trim();
        if (!text) return;
                                
        $chatInput.val('').prop('disabled', true);
        $sendButton.prop('disabled', true);
                 
        try {
        const tId = parseInt(currentTicketId, 10);
        const kId = currentTicketData.idKhachHang ? parseInt(currentTicketData.idKhachHang, 10) : null;
        const gId = currentTicketData.guestSessionId || null;
                                        
        await hubConnection.invoke("SendMessageFromStaff", currentGroupName, text, tId, kId, gId);
        $('#chatHeaderStatus').text('Đã trả lời');
        } catch (err) {
        Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Không thể gửi tin nhắn: ' + err.message, 'error');
        } finally {
        $chatInput.prop('disabled', false).focus();
        $sendButton.prop('disabled', false);
        }
        });

        // ĐÓNG PHIẾU
        $resolveButton.on('click', async function () {
        if (!currentTicketId) return;
                        
        const confirmRes = await Swal.fire({
        title: 'Xác nhận xử lý?',
        text: "Bạn có chắc chắn phiếu hỗ trợ này đã được giải quyết?",
        icon: 'question',
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonColor: '#2E7D32'
        });

        if (confirmRes.isConfirmed) {
        try {
        const res = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/nhanvien/hotro/resolve/${currentTicketId}`, { method: 'POST', headers: headers });
        if (res.ok) {
        Swal.fire({toast: true, position: 'top-end', icon: 'success', title: 'Đã đóng phiếu!', showConfirmButton: false, timer: 1500});
                            
        loadTicketList(false); // Cập nhật lại danh sách phiếu
                            
        $('#chat-header').css('visibility', 'hidden');
        $chatHistory.html('<div class="h-100 d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center text-muted"><p>Phiếu đã đóng.</p></div>');
        $chatInput.prop('disabled', true);
        $sendButton.prop('disabled', true);
        $resolveButton.prop('disabled', true);
        currentTicketId = null;
        }
        } catch (err) { Swal.fire("Lỗi", "Lỗi xử lý.", "error"); }
        }
        });

        // Mobile view buttons
        $('#btnBackToList').click(() => $('#mainDashboard').removeClass('show-chat'));
        $('#btnShowSummary').click(() => $('#mainDashboard').addClass('show-summary'));
        $('#btnBackToChat').click(() => $('#mainDashboard').removeClass('show-summary'));

        // Khởi động
        startConnection();
        loadTicketList(false);
        });
    </script>
}

FILE: E:/Tai Lieu Hoc Tap/N19 KLTN 032026/Cafebook/WebCafebookApi/Pages\Employee\HoTroKhachHangView.cshtml.cs
================================================================================
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class HoTroKhachHangViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IConfiguration _configuration;

        public HoTroKhachHangViewModel(IConfiguration configuration)
        {
            _configuration = configuration;
        }

        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = "";
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public IActionResult OnGet()
        {
            string? url = _configuration.GetSection("ApiSettings")["BaseUrl"];
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(url)) url = _configuration["ApiBaseUrl"];

            ApiBaseUrl = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(url) ? "http://localhost:5202" : url.TrimEnd('/');

            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken))
            {
                string currentUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString;
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = currentUrl });
            }

            return Page(); 
        }
    }
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";
        
        let _allReviews = [];
        let _allFeedbacks = [];
        
        let _currentReviewId = null;
        let _currentFeedbackId = null;

        // ================= ĐÁNH GIÁ SẢN PHẨM =================
        async function loadReviews() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/reviews`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
                _allReviews = await res.json();
                
                calculateAverageRating();
                renderReviews();
            } catch (err) {
                console.error("Lỗi tải đánh giá:", err);
            }
        }

        function calculateAverageRating() {
            if (_allReviews.length === 0) {
                $("#lblAvgRating").text("0.0");
                $("#lblTotalReviews").text("Chưa có đánh giá nào");
                $("#starsAvgContainer").html('<span class="material-symbols-outlined">star_outline</span>'.repeat(5));
                return;
            }

            const totalStars = _allReviews.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.soSao, 0);
            const avg = (totalStars / _allReviews.length).toFixed(1);
            
            $("#lblAvgRating").text(avg);
            $("#lblTotalReviews").text(`${_allReviews.length} đánh giá từ khách hàng`);

            let starsHtml = '';
            for(let i=1; i<=5; i++) {
                if (i <= Math.floor(avg)) starsHtml += '<span class="material-symbols-outlined">star</span>';
                else if (i - 0.5 <= avg) starsHtml += '<span class="material-symbols-outlined">star_half</span>';
                else starsHtml += '<span class="material-symbols-outlined">star_outline</span>';
            }
            $("#starsAvgContainer").html(starsHtml);
        }

        function renderReviews() {
            const searchTerm = $("#searchReview").val().toLowerCase();
            const hideReplied = $("#chkUnrepliedReview").is(':checked');
            
            let filtered = _allReviews;

            // 1. Lọc theo trạng thái phản hồi
            if (hideReplied) {
                filtered = filtered.filter(r => !r.danhSachPhanHoi || r.danhSachPhanHoi.length === 0);
            }

            // 2. Lọc theo text search
            if (searchTerm) {
                filtered = filtered.filter(r =>
                    (r.tenKhachHang && r.tenKhachHang.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm)) ||
                    (r.tenSanPham && r.tenSanPham.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm)) ||
                    (r.binhLuan && r.binhLuan.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm))
                );
            }

            const $list = $("#review-list").empty();

            if(filtered.length === 0) {
                $list.html(`<div class="col-12 text-center py-5 text-muted"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 mb-3">inbox</span><br/>Không tìm thấy đánh giá nào phù hợp.</div>`);
                return;
            }

            filtered.forEach((d, index) => {
                const delay = (index % 10) * 0.05; // Tạo hiệu ứng xuất hiện lần lượt
                let stars = '';
                for(let i=1; i<=5; i++) stars += `<span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-5 ${i <= d.soSao ? 'text-warning' : 'text-light'}">star</span>`;
                
                let repliesHtml = d.danhSachPhanHoi.map(p => `
                    <div class="phkh-reply-item mt-3">
                        <div class="fw-bold small text-primary-coffee mb-1"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">support_agent</span> ${p.tenNhanVien} <span class="text-muted fw-normal float-end">${new Date(p.ngayTao).toLocaleString()}</span></div>
                        <div class="small">${p.noiDung}</div>
                    </div>
                `).join('');
                
                let imageHtml = d.hinhAnhUrl ? `
                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <a href="${d.hinhAnhUrl}" target="_blank" title="Nhấn để xem ảnh gốc">
                            <img src="${d.hinhAnhUrl}" class="phkh-review-img border shadow-sm" alt="Ảnh đánh giá">
                        </a>
                    </div>
                ` : '';

                const hasReplied = d.danhSachPhanHoi && d.danhSachPhanHoi.length > 0;

                $list.append(`
                    <div class="col-md-6 col-xl-4 anim-item" style="animation-delay: ${delay}s">
                        <div class="card phkh-review-card h-100 bg-white">
                            <div class="card-body p-4 d-flex flex-column">
                                <div class="d-flex justify-content-between mb-2 align-items-center">
                                    <h6 class="fw-bold text-dark m-0 text-truncate" title="${d.tenKhachHang}">${d.tenKhachHang}</h6>
                                    <div class="phkh-stars d-flex">${stars}</div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="badge bg-primary-coffee align-self-start mb-3 px-3 py-2 rounded-pill">${d.tenSanPham}</div>
                                
                                ${imageHtml}
                                
                                <p class="text-muted small mb-3 flex-grow-1">${d.binhLuan || '<i>Không có bình luận</i>'}</p>
                                
                                <div class="phkh-replies-area mb-3">${repliesHtml}</div>
                                
                                <div class="d-flex gap-2 mt-auto">
                                    <button class="btn ${hasReplied ? 'btn-outline-secondary' : 'btn-outline-coffee'} btn-sm flex-grow-1 rounded-pill fw-medium" onclick="openReplyModal(${d.idDanhGia})">
                                        ${hasReplied ? 'Phản hồi thêm' : 'Phản hồi ngay'}
                                    </button>
                                    <button class="btn ${d.trangThai === 'Hiển thị' ? 'btn-outline-danger' : 'btn-outline-success'} btn-sm rounded-pill" onclick="toggleReview(${d.idDanhGia})" title="${d.trangThai === 'Hiển thị' ? 'Ẩn đánh giá này trên App' : 'Hiện lại đánh giá này'}">
                                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle fs-5">${d.trangThai === 'Hiển thị' ? 'visibility_off' : 'visibility'}</span>
                                    </button>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `);
            });
        }

        // ================= GÓP Ý HỆ THỐNG =================
        async function loadFeedbacks() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/feedbacks`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
                _allFeedbacks = await res.json();
                renderFeedbacks();
            } catch(err) {
                console.error("Lỗi tải góp ý:", err);
            }
        }

        function renderFeedbacks() {
            const searchTerm = $("#searchFeedback").val().toLowerCase();
            
            let filtered = _allFeedbacks;
            if (searchTerm) {
                filtered = filtered.filter(g =>
                    (g.hoTen && g.hoTen.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm)) ||
                    (g.email && g.email.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm)) ||
                    (g.noiDung && g.noiDung.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm))
                );
            }

            const $pendingBody = $("#feedback-pending-body").empty();
            const $historyBody = $("#feedback-history-body").empty();

            let pendingCount = 0;
            let historyCount = 0;

            filtered.forEach(g => {
                const dateStr = new Date(g.ngayTao).toLocaleString('vi-VN', {hour: '2-digit', minute:'2-digit', day:'2-digit', month:'2-digit', year:'numeric'});
                
                if (g.trangThai === 'Chờ xử lý') {
                    pendingCount++;
                    const safeGopY = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(g));
                    $pendingBody.append(`
                        <tr class="anim-item">
                            <td class="ps-4"><div class="fw-bold text-dark">${g.hoTen}</div><div class="small text-muted">${g.email}</div></td>
                            <td><div class="text-wrap fw-medium" style="min-width: 250px; max-width: 400px;">${g.noiDung}</div></td>
                            <td><div class="small text-muted"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">schedule</span> ${dateStr}</div></td>
                            <td class="text-center pe-4">
                                <button class="btn btn-primary-coffee btn-sm rounded-pill px-3 fw-bold shadow-sm" onclick="openFeedbackEmailModal('${safeGopY}')">Xử lý Email</button>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    `);
                } else {
                    historyCount++;
                    $historyBody.append(`
                        <tr class="anim-item">
                            <td class="ps-4"><div class="fw-bold text-dark">${g.hoTen}</div><div class="small text-muted">${g.email}</div></td>
                            <td><div class="text-wrap text-muted" style="min-width: 250px; max-width: 400px;">${g.noiDung}</div></td>
                            <td><div class="small text-muted">${dateStr}</div></td>
                            <td class="text-center pe-4"><span class="badge bg-success-subtle text-success border border-success-subtle px-3 py-2 rounded-pill"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">done_all</span> ${g.trangThai}</span></td>
                        </tr>
                    `);
                }
            });

            if(pendingCount === 0) $pendingBody.html('<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center py-5 text-muted fst-italic"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 mb-2">task_alt</span><br/>Tuyệt vời! Không có góp ý nào đang chờ xử lý.</td></tr>');
            if(historyCount === 0) $historyBody.html('<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center py-5 text-muted fst-italic">Chưa có lịch sử xử lý.</td></tr>');
        }

        // ================= EVENTS LỌC TÌM KIẾM =================
        $("#searchReview").on("input", renderReviews);
        $("#chkUnrepliedReview").on("change", renderReviews);
        $("#searchFeedback").on("input", renderFeedbacks);

        // ================= ACTIONS & MODALS =================
        function openReplyModal(id) {
            _currentReviewId = id;
            $("#replyText").val('');
            $("#replyModal").modal('show');
        }

        $("#btnConfirmReply").click(async () => {
            const content = $("#replyText").val().trim();
            if(!content) return;
            
            const btn = $("#btnConfirmReply");
            btn.prop('disabled', true).html('<span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span> Đang gửi...');

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/reply-review/${_currentReviewId}`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ noiDung: content })
                });
                if(res.ok) {
                    $("#replyModal").modal('hide');
                    Swal.fire('Thành công', 'Đã phản hồi khách hàng', 'success');
                    await loadReviews();
                }
            } finally {
                btn.prop('disabled', false).text('GỬI PHẢN HỒI LÊN APP');
            }
        });

        async function toggleReview(id) {
            const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/toggle-review/${id}`, { method: 'PUT', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
            if(res.ok) loadReviews();
        }

        window.openFeedbackEmailModal = function(encodedData) {
            const g = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(encodedData));
            _currentFeedbackId = g.idGopY;
            $("#fb-customer-info").html(`Gửi tới: <strong class="text-dark">${g.hoTen}</strong> (${g.email})`);
            $("#fb-original-content").text(`Nội dung khách gửi: "${g.noiDung}"`);
            $("#feedbackEmailText").val('');
            $("#feedbackEmailModal").modal('show');
        };

        $("#btnAutoTemplate").click(function() {
            const template = "Cảm ơn bạn đã đóng góp ý kiến để giúp hệ thống ngày một hoàn thiện hơn. Chúng tôi đã ghi nhận phản hồi của bạn và sẽ tiến hành khắc phục/cải thiện trong thời gian sớm nhất.\n\nChúc bạn một ngày làm việc tràn đầy năng lượng cùng Cafebook!";
            $("#feedbackEmailText").val(template);
        });

        $("#btnSendFeedbackEmail").click(async function() {
            const content = $("#feedbackEmailText").val().trim();
            if(!content) return Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Vui lòng nhập nội dung email', 'warning');

            $("#feedbackEmailModal").modal('hide');
            Swal.fire({
                title: 'Đang gửi Email...',
                html: 'Vui lòng không đóng trình duyệt lúc này.',
                allowOutsideClick: false,
                didOpen: () => { Swal.showLoading(); }
            });

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/reply-feedback/${_currentFeedbackId}`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ NoiDungEmail: content })
                });

                if(res.ok) {
                    Swal.fire('Thành công', 'Đã gửi email phản hồi và đóng góp ý!', 'success');
                    await loadFeedbacks();
                } else {
                    const err = await res.json();
                    Swal.fire('Lỗi gửi mail', err.message, 'error');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Mất kết nối máy chủ', 'error');
            }
        });

        $(document).ready(() => {
            $("#feedbackEmailModal, #replyModal").appendTo("body");

            loadReviews();
            loadFeedbacks();
        });
    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class PhanHoiKhachHangViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public PhanHoiKhachHangViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet()
        {
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken))
            {
                string currentUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString;
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = currentUrl });
            }

            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/PhanHoiKhachHangWeb";

            return Page(); 
        }
    }
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";
        let _currentCodOrderId = null;
        let _currentCodTotal = 0;

        const formatVND = (num) => new Intl.NumberFormat('vi-VN', { style: 'currency', currency: 'VND' }).format(num);

        // Hàm load dữ liệu chính
        async function loadOrders() {
            try {
                // 1. Load đơn hàng sẵn sàng
                const resAvail = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/available-orders`, {
                    headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    cache: 'no-store'
                });
                if(resAvail.ok) renderList(await resAvail.json(), "#available-list", true);

                // 2. Load đơn hàng đang giao của tôi
                const resMy = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/my-orders`, {
                    headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    cache: 'no-store'
                });
                if(resMy.ok) renderList(await resMy.json(), "#active-list", false);

                // 3. Load tổng hợp lịch sử
                const resHistory = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/history-summary`, {
                    headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    cache: 'no-store'
                });
                if(resHistory.ok) renderHistory(await resHistory.json());
                
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Lỗi load dữ liệu:", error);
            }
        }

        // Hàm Render danh sách đơn hàng (Sửa lỗi khớp với UI mới)
        function renderList(data, containerId, isNew) {
            const $cont = $(containerId).empty();
            
            if (!data || data.length === 0) {
                return $cont.html('<div class="col-12 text-center p-5 text-muted fst-italic">Hiện không có đơn hàng nào cần xử lý.</div>');
            }
    
            data.forEach(d => {
                // Kiểm tra điều kiện COD [cite: 150]
                const isCod = (d.phuongThucThanhToan === "COD" || d.phuongThucThanhToan === "Tiền mặt") && d.trangThaiThanhToan !== "Đã thanh toán";
                
                // Badge phương thức thanh toán [cite: 151]
                const pttBadge = isCod
                    ? '<span class="badge badge-cod rounded-pill px-3 py-2"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle me-1">payments</span> Thu COD</span>'
                    : '<span class="badge badge-paid rounded-pill px-3 py-2"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle me-1">check_circle</span> Đã thanh toán</span>';

                // Nút bấm thao tác [cite: 152, 153]
                const actionBtn = isNew
                    ? `<button class="btn btn-primary-coffee w-100 rounded-pill fw-bold py-3 shadow-sm material-ripple" onclick="acceptOrder(${d.idHoaDon})">NHẬN GIAO ĐƠN NÀY</button>`
                    : `<div class="d-flex gap-2">
                        <button class="btn btn-success flex-grow-1 rounded-pill fw-bold py-3 shadow-sm material-ripple" onclick="triggerCompleteOrder(${d.idHoaDon}, ${isCod}, ${d.thanhTien})">GIAO XONG</button>
                        <button class="btn btn-outline-danger rounded-pill px-3 material-ripple" onclick="failOrder(${d.idHoaDon})"><span class="material-symbols-outlined">close</span></button>
                       </div>`;

                // Append Card vào container với cấu trúc UI mới [cite: 155, 157, 158, 159, 160]
                $cont.append(`
                    <div class="col-12 col-md-6 col-lg-4">
                        <div class="card sgh-card shadow-sm h-100">
                            <div class="card-body p-4">
                                <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-start mb-3">
                                    <span class="badge bg-light text-dark border rounded-pill px-3">#${d.idHoaDon}</span>
                                    <div class="text-end">
                                        <div class="fw-black text-accent fs-4">${formatVND(d.thanhTien)}</div>
                                        <button class="btn btn-sm btn-link text-primary p-0 text-decoration-none small" onclick="openOrderDetails(${d.idHoaDon})">Xem chi tiết món</button>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="mb-3">${pttBadge}</div>
                                <h5 class="fw-bold text-dark mb-2">${d.tenKhachHang}</h5>
                                <div class="d-flex align-items-center mb-2 small">
                                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 me-2 text-primary">call</span>
                                    <a href="tel:${d.soDienThoai}" class="text-decoration-none fw-bold text-primary">${d.soDienThoai}</a>
                                </div>
                                <div class="d-flex align-items-start mb-4 small">
                                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 me-2 text-primary">location_on</span>
                                    <span class="text-muted">${d.diaChi}</span>
                                </div>
                                ${actionBtn}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `);
            });
        }

        // Hàm Render lịch sử và đối soát [cite: 163, 164, 165, 166, 168]
        function renderHistory(summary) {
            $("#summaryTotalMoney").text(formatVND(summary.tongTienMatCam));
            $("#summarySuccess").text(summary.tongDonHoanThanh);
            $("#summaryFail").text(summary.tongDonHuy);
            
            const $list = $("#history-list").empty();
            if(!summary.lichSuDonHang || summary.lichSuDonHang.length === 0) {
                return $list.html('<div class="text-center p-4 text-muted fst-italic">Chưa có lịch sử giao hàng hôm nay.</div>');
            }

            summary.lichSuDonHang.forEach(d => {
                const isSuccess = d.trangThaiGiaoHang === "Hoàn thành";
                const badge = isSuccess ? '<span class="badge bg-success">Thành công</span>' : '<span class="badge bg-danger">Đã hủy</span>';
                const time = new Date(d.thoiGianTao).toLocaleTimeString('vi-VN', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
                const isCod = (d.phuongThucThanhToan === "COD" || d.phuongThucThanhToan === "Tiền mặt");

                $list.append(`
                    <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-3">
                        <div class="card-body p-3 d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                            <div>
                                <div class="fw-bold text-dark">#${d.idHoaDon} - ${d.tenKhachHang}</div>
                                <div class="small text-muted"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">schedule</span> ${time} | ${badge}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="text-end">
                                <div class="fw-bold ${isSuccess ? 'text-success' : 'text-muted text-decoration-line-through'}">${formatVND(d.thanhTien)}</div>
                                <div class="small text-muted">${isCod ? 'Tiền mặt' : d.phuongThucThanhToan}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `);
            });
        }

        // --- Các hàm xử lý Logic nghiệp vụ (Giữ nguyên logic của bạn) ---

        async function openOrderDetails(idHoaDon) {
            $("#detail-items-body").html('<tr><td colspan="3" class="text-center p-4"><div class="spinner-border text-primary"></div></td></tr>');
            $("#orderDetailModal").modal('show');
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/order-details/${idHoaDon}`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
                const data = await res.json();
                const $body = $("#detail-items-body").empty();
                data.forEach(item => {
                    $body.append(`
                        <tr>
                            <td class="ps-0">
                                <div class="fw-bold text-dark">${item.tenSanPham}</div>
                                ${item.ghiChuMon ? `<div class="small text-primary fst-italic">${item.ghiChuMon}</div>` : ''}
                            </td>
                            <td class="text-center fw-bold">x${item.soLuong}</td>
                            <td class="text-end pe-0 fw-medium">${formatVND(item.thanhTien)}</td>
                        </tr>
                    `);
                });
            } catch(e) { $("#detail-items-body").html('<tr><td colspan="3" class="text-center text-danger">Lỗi tải dữ liệu.</td></tr>'); }
        }

        async function acceptOrder(id) {
            const formData = new FormData(); formData.append("tacVu", "NhanDon");
            const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/update-status/${id}`, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` }, body: formData });
            if(res.ok) {
                Swal.fire({ title: 'Đã nhận đơn', icon: 'success', toast: true, position: 'top-end', timer: 1500, showConfirmButton: false });
                loadOrders();
            }
        }

        function triggerCompleteOrder(id, isCod, totalAmount) {
            if(isCod) {
                _currentCodOrderId = id; _currentCodTotal = totalAmount;
                openCodCalculator(totalAmount);
            } else {
                captureProofAndSubmit(id);
            }
        }

        function openCodCalculator(total) {
            $("#codTotalAmount").text(formatVND(total));
            $("#codCustomerGiven").val("");
            $("#codChangeAmount").text("0 đ").removeClass("text-danger").addClass("text-success");
            $("#btnConfirmCod").prop("disabled", true);
            
            const $btns = $("#codQuickButtons").empty();
            const presets = [total, 100000, 200000, 500000].filter((v, i, a) => v >= total && a.indexOf(v) === i).sort((a,b) => a-b);
            presets.forEach(p => {
                let label = p === total ? "Đưa Đủ" : (p/1000 + "K");
                $btns.append(`<div class="col-3"><button class="btn btn-outline-secondary w-100 fw-bold px-0 btn-quick-cash" data-val="${p}">${label}</button></div>`);
            });
            $("#codModal").modal('show');
        }

        $("#codCustomerGiven").on('input', function() {
            let val = $(this).val().replace(/\D/g, '');
            let given = parseInt(val || 0);
            $(this).val(given === 0 ? '' : given.toLocaleString('vi-VN'));
            calculateChange(given);
        });

        $("#codQuickButtons").on("click", ".btn-quick-cash", function() {
            let given = parseInt($(this).data("val"));
            $("#codCustomerGiven").val(given.toLocaleString('vi-VN'));
            calculateChange(given);
        });

        function calculateChange(given) {
            let change = given - _currentCodTotal;
            if (change < 0) {
                $("#codChangeAmount").text(`Thiếu: ${formatVND(Math.abs(change))}`).removeClass("text-success").addClass("text-danger");
                $("#btnConfirmCod").prop("disabled", true);
            } else {
                $("#codChangeAmount").text(formatVND(change)).removeClass("text-danger").addClass("text-success");
                $("#btnConfirmCod").prop("disabled", false);
            }
        }

        $("#btnConfirmCod").click(function() {
            $("#codModal").modal('hide');
            setTimeout(() => { captureProofAndSubmit(_currentCodOrderId); }, 400);
        });

        async function captureProofAndSubmit(id) {
            const { value: file } = await Swal.fire({
                title: 'Chụp ảnh xác nhận', text: 'Hãy chụp gói hàng để làm bằng chứng giao thành công.', input: 'file',
                inputAttributes: { 'accept': 'image/*', 'capture': 'environment' },
                showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonText: 'Xác Nhận Giao Xong', confirmButtonColor: '#4CAF50'
            });

            if (file) {
                Swal.fire({ title: 'Đang xử lý...', allowOutsideClick: false, didOpen: () => Swal.showLoading() });
                const formData = new FormData();
                formData.append("tacVu", "HoanThanh");
                formData.append("proofImage", file);
                try {
                    const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/update-status/${id}`, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` }, body: formData });
                    if(res.ok) {
                        Swal.fire('Thành công!', 'Đơn hàng hoàn tất.', 'success');
                        loadOrders();
                    } else {
                        Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Cập nhật thất bại.', 'error');
                    }
                } catch(e) { Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Lỗi kết nối mạng.', 'error'); }
            }
        }

        async function failOrder(id) {
            const { value: reason } = await Swal.fire({
                title: 'Lý do hủy đơn?',
                input: 'text',
                inputPlaceholder: 'Khách không nghe máy, boom hàng...',
                showCancelButton: true,
                confirmButtonColor: '#d33'
            });
            if (reason) {
                const formData = new FormData();
                formData.append("tacVu", "Huy");
                formData.append("lyDoHuy", reason);
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/update-status/${id}`, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` }, body: formData });
                if(res.ok) loadOrders();
            }
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
            $('#orderDetailModal').appendTo("body");
            $('#codModal').appendTo("body");
            loadOrders();
        });
    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class ShipperGiaoHangViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;

        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public ShipperGiaoHangViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet()
        {
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken))
            {
                string currentUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString;
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = currentUrl });
            }

            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/giaohangweb";

            return Page();
        }
    }
}

@section Styles {
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/SoDoBan.css" asp-append-version="true" />

<div class="container-fluid px-0 px-md-2 fade-in-up">
    
    <div class="sdb-header-actions d-flex flex-wrap justify-content-between align-items-center mb-3 gap-3">
        <div class="d-flex align-items-center gap-3">
            <h2 class="fw-bold m-0 text-primary-dark">@ViewData["Title"]</h2>
            <button id="btn-tao-don-mang-ve" class="btn btn-accent material-ripple d-flex align-items-center gap-2 shadow-sm rounded-pill px-4">
                <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-5">takeout_dining</span>
                <span class="d-none d-sm-inline fw-bold">Đơn Tại Quầy / Mang Về</span>
                <span class="d-inline d-sm-none fw-bold">Mang Về</span>
            </button>
        </div>

        <div class="sdb-legend d-none d-md-flex small fw-medium gap-3">
            <div class="legend-item"><span class="sdb-status-box bg-trong"></span> Trống</div>
            <div class="legend-item"><span class="sdb-status-box bg-co-khach"></span> Có khách</div>

            <div class="legend-item"><span class="sdb-status-box bg-bao-tri"></span> Bảo trì</div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="row g-3">
        
        <div class="col-12 col-lg-2 col-xl-2">
            <nav class="sdb-khuvuc-tabs card shadow-sm border-0 h-100">
                <div class="card-body p-2 p-lg-3">
                    <h6 class="p-2 text-muted text-uppercase fw-bold small mb-2 d-none d-lg-block">Khu Vực</h6>
                    <ul class="nav nav-pills flex-row flex-lg-column sdb-nav-mobile-scroll" id="khuvuc-nav">
                        <li class="nav-item">
                            <a class="nav-link active material-ripple" href="#" data-khuvuc-id="all">
                                <span class="material-symbols-outlined icon-sm">apps</span> Tất cả
                            </a>
                        </li>
                        <li class="nav-item d-none d-lg-block"><hr class="my-2 mx-3 border-secondary"></li>
                        @foreach (var kv in Model.KhuVucList)
                        {
                            <li class="nav-item">
                                <a class="nav-link material-ripple" href="#" data-khuvuc-id="@kv.IdKhuVuc">
                                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined icon-sm">label</span> @kv.TenKhuVuc
                                </a>
                            </li>
                        }
                    </ul>
                </div>
            </nav>
        </div>

        <div class="col-12 col-lg-6 col-xl-7">
            <div id="table-layout-container" class="sdb-grid pb-5 pb-lg-0">
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="col-12 col-lg-4 col-xl-3 sdb-panel-wrapper">
            <div class="sdb-panel-drag-handle d-lg-none" onclick="resetPanel()">
                <span></span>
            </div>

            <div class="card shadow-sm border-0 sdb-action-panel sticky-lg-top" style="top: 20px;">
                <div class="card-body p-4">
                    
                    <div id="panel-no-selection" class="text-center py-5">
                        <div class="icon-circle mx-auto mb-3"><span class="material-symbols-outlined text-muted" style="font-size: 40px;">touch_app</span></div>
                        <h5 class="fw-bold text-primary-dark">Chưa chọn bàn</h5>
                        <p class="text-muted small">Chạm vào một bàn trên sơ đồ để thao tác</p>
                    </div>

                    <div id="panel-selection-mode" class="text-center py-4" style="display: none;">
                        <h5 id="selection-text-header" class="fw-bold text-accent">...</h5>
                        <p class="text-muted small mb-4">Vui lòng chọn bàn đích trên sơ đồ</p>
                        <button id="btn-cancel-select" class="btn btn-outline-danger w-100 rounded-pill material-ripple fw-bold">
                            <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle">close</span> Hủy Thao Tác
                        </button>
                    </div>

                    <div id="panel-da-chon" style="display: none;">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-start mb-3">
                            <div>
                                <span class="text-muted fw-bold small text-uppercase letter-spacing-1">Bàn Đang Chọn</span>
                                <h2 class="fw-bold m-0 text-primary-dark">Bàn <span id="ban-so-ban"></span></h2>
                            </div>
                            <span id="ban-trang-thai" class="badge fs-6 rounded-pill px-3 py-2 mt-1 shadow-sm">Trống</span>
                        </div>

                        <div id="ban-dat-truoc-group" class="sdb-alert alert-warning" style="display:none;">
                            <span class="material-symbols-outlined">bookmark_added</span>
                            <span id="ban-thong-tin-dat-ban" class="fw-bold small"></span>
                        </div>

                        <div id="ban-ghi-chu-group" class="sdb-alert alert-secondary" style="display:none;">
                            <span class="material-symbols-outlined">info</span>
                            <span class="small"><strong class="text-dark">Ghi chú:</strong> <span id="ban-ghi-chu"></span></span>
                        </div>

                        <div id="ban-tong-tien-group" class="sdb-price-box text-center my-3" style="display:none;">
                            <span class="text-muted small fw-bold d-block mb-1">TỔNG TIỀN TẠM TÍNH</span>
                            <h3 id="ban-tong-tien" class="text-accent fw-black m-0">0 đ</h3>
                        </div>

                        <hr class="my-4 border-secondary opacity-25" />

                        <div class="d-grid gap-3">
                            <button id="btn-goi-mon-cu" class="btn btn-primary-theme btn-lg rounded-4 fw-bold d-flex justify-content-center align-items-center gap-2 material-ripple shadow-sm">
                                <span class="material-symbols-outlined">add_shopping_cart</span>
                                <span id="btn-goi-mon-text-main">Gọi Món</span>
                            </button>

                            <div class="row g-2 mt-0">
                                <div class="col-6 d-grid">
                                    <button id="btn-chuyen-ban" class="btn btn-outline-secondary-theme rounded-4 fw-bold d-flex flex-column align-items-center py-2 material-ripple">
                                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-4 mb-1">swap_horiz</span> Chuyển Bàn
                                    </button>
                                </div>
                                <div class="col-6 d-grid">
                                    <button id="btn-gop-ban" class="btn btn-outline-secondary-theme rounded-4 fw-bold d-flex flex-column align-items-center py-2 material-ripple">
                                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-4 mb-1">merge_type</span> Gộp Bàn
                                    </button>
                                </div>
                            </div>

                            <button id="btn-bao-cao-su-co" class="btn btn-subtle-danger rounded-pill mt-2 fw-bold material-ripple">
                                <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle">warning</span> Báo cáo Sự cố
                            </button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<div class="sdb-mobile-overlay d-lg-none" onclick="resetPanel()"></div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";
        let allTables = [];
        let currentSelectedBan = null;
        let currentMode = "none";
        let sourceHoaDonId = null;

        async function redirectToGoiMonSecure(idHoaDon) {
            const response = await fetch(`/nhan-vien/so-do-ban?handler=EncryptUrl&id=${idHoaDon}`);
            const data = await response.json();
            window.location.href = data.url;
        }

        const formatCurrency = (number) => new Intl.NumberFormat('vi-VN', { style: 'currency', currency: 'VND' }).format(number);

        async function loadTables() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/tables`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${jwtToken}` }});
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Lỗi tải sơ đồ");
                allTables = await response.json();
                renderTables(allTables);
            } catch (err) {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi', err.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        function renderTables(banList) {
            const $container = $("#table-layout-container").empty();
            if (!banList || banList.length === 0) return $container.html('<p class="text-center w-100 p-5 text-muted">Khu vực này trống.</p>');
            
            banList.forEach(ban => {
                let statusClass = "sdb-card-trong", icon = "deck";
                let infoHtml = `<div class="sdb-table-status">${ban.trangThai}</div>`;

                if (ban.trangThai === "Có khách") {
                    statusClass = "sdb-card-co-khach";
                    icon = "local_cafe";
                    infoHtml = `<div class="sdb-table-price">${formatCurrency(ban.tongTienHienTai)}</div>`;
                }
                else if (ban.trangThai === "Đã đặt") { statusClass = "sdb-card-da-dat"; icon = "book_online"; }
                else if (ban.trangThai === "Bảo trì") { statusClass = "sdb-card-bao-tri"; icon = "build"; }

                const cardHtml = `
                    <div class="sdb-table-card ${statusClass} material-ripple-subtle" data-ban-id="${ban.idBan}">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-start w-100 mb-2">
                            <h4 class="sdb-table-name">${ban.soBan}</h4>
                            <div class="sdb-table-icon"><span class="material-symbols-outlined">${icon}</span></div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="mt-auto w-100 text-start">
                            ${infoHtml}
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                $container.append(cardHtml);
            });
        }

        async function callApiAction(endpoint, payload, successMsg) {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/${endpoint}`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${jwtToken}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
                });
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error(await response.text());
                
                await Swal.fire({title: 'Thành công!', text: successMsg, icon: 'success', confirmButtonColor: '#5D4037'});
                resetPanel();
                loadTables();
            } catch (error) {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi Thao Tác', error.message, 'error');
            }
        }

        function updatePanel(banId) {
            currentSelectedBan = allTables.find(b => b.idBan == banId);
            if(!currentSelectedBan) return;

            $(".sdb-panel-wrapper").addClass("active-mobile");
            $(".sdb-mobile-overlay").addClass("show");

            $("#panel-no-selection, #panel-selection-mode").hide();
            $("#panel-da-chon").show();
            $("#ban-so-ban").text(currentSelectedBan.soBan);
            $("#ban-trang-thai").text(currentSelectedBan.trangThai).removeClass().addClass('badge fs-6 rounded-pill px-3 py-2 mt-1 shadow-sm');
            
            $("#ban-dat-truoc-group, #ban-ghi-chu-group, #ban-tong-tien-group").hide();
            $("#btn-chuyen-ban, #btn-gop-ban").hide();
            $("#btn-bao-cao-su-co").text("Báo cáo Sự cố").prepend('<span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-1">warning</span>');

            const status = currentSelectedBan.trangThai;
            if (status === "Trống") {
                $("#ban-trang-thai").addClass('bg-success text-white');
                $("#btn-goi-mon-cu").show().find('span:last').text("Tạo Hóa Đơn");
            } else if (status === "Có khách") {
                $("#ban-trang-thai").addClass('bg-accent text-white');
                $("#ban-tong-tien-group, #btn-chuyen-ban, #btn-gop-ban").show();
                $("#ban-tong-tien").text(formatCurrency(currentSelectedBan.tongTienHienTai));
                $("#btn-goi-mon-cu").show().find('span:last').text("Chi tiết / Thanh toán");
            } else if (status === "Đã đặt") {
                $("#ban-trang-thai").addClass('bg-warning text-dark');
                $("#ban-dat-truoc-group").show();
                $("#ban-thong-tin-dat-ban").text(currentSelectedBan.thongTinDatBan);
                $("#btn-goi-mon-cu").show().find('span:last').text("Khách đến (Mở bàn)");
            } else if (status === "Bảo trì") {
                $("#ban-trang-thai").addClass('bg-secondary text-white');
                if (currentSelectedBan.ghiChu) { $("#ban-ghi-chu-group").show(); $("#ban-ghi-chu").text(currentSelectedBan.ghiChu); }
                $("#btn-goi-mon-cu").hide();
                $("#btn-bao-cao-su-co").text("Mở lại bàn").prepend('<span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-1">build_circle</span>');
            }
        }

        function resetPanel() {
            currentMode = "none";
            currentSelectedBan = null; sourceHoaDonId = null;
            
            $(".sdb-panel-wrapper").removeClass("active-mobile");
            $(".sdb-mobile-overlay").removeClass("show");

            setTimeout(() => {
                $("#panel-no-selection").show(); $("#panel-da-chon, #panel-selection-mode").hide();
            }, 300); 

            $(".sdb-table-card").removeClass("selected dimmed");
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
            loadTables();

            $("#khuvuc-nav").on("click", ".nav-link", function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $("#khuvuc-nav .nav-link").removeClass("active"); $(this).addClass("active");
                const kvId = $(this).data("khuvuc-id");
                renderTables(kvId === "all" ? allTables : allTables.filter(b => b.idKhuVuc == kvId));
                resetPanel();
            });

            $("#table-layout-container").on("click", ".sdb-table-card", function() {
                if ($(this).hasClass("dimmed")) return;
                const banId = $(this).data("ban-id");
                
                if (currentMode === "none") {
                    $(".sdb-table-card").removeClass("selected"); $(this).addClass("selected");
                    updatePanel(banId);
                } else {
                    const targetBan = allTables.find(b => b.idBan == banId);
                    if (currentMode === 'chuyen' && targetBan.trangThai !== 'Trống') return Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Bàn đích phải trống', 'warning');
                    if (currentMode === 'gop' && targetBan.trangThai !== 'Có khách') return Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Chỉ có thể gộp vào bàn đang có khách', 'warning');
                    if (targetBan.idBan === currentSelectedBan.idBan) return Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Không thể thao tác với chính nó', 'warning');
                    
                    Swal.fire({
                        title: 'Xác nhận thao tác',
                        text: `Xác nhận ${currentMode === 'chuyen' ? 'CHUYỂN' : 'GỘP'} từ Bàn ${currentSelectedBan.soBan} -> Bàn ${targetBan.soBan}?`,
                        icon: 'question', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#5D4037', confirmButtonText: 'Đồng ý'
                    }).then((result) => {
                        if (result.isConfirmed) {
                            const endpoint = currentMode === 'chuyen' ? 'move-table' : 'merge-table';
                            callApiAction(endpoint, { idHoaDonNguon: sourceHoaDonId, idBanDich: targetBan.idBan, idHoaDonDich: targetBan.idHoaDonHienTai }, 'Thao tác thành công!');
                        }
                    });
                }
            });

            $("#btn-chuyen-ban, #btn-gop-ban").click(function() {
                currentMode = this.id.includes('chuyen') ? 'chuyen' : 'gop';
                sourceHoaDonId = currentSelectedBan.idHoaDonHienTai;
                $("#panel-da-chon").hide(); $("#panel-selection-mode").show();
                $("#selection-text-header").text(`Đang ${currentMode === 'chuyen' ? 'Chuyển' : 'Gộp'} Bàn ${currentSelectedBan.soBan}`);
                
                $(".sdb-panel-wrapper").removeClass("active-mobile");
                $(".sdb-mobile-overlay").removeClass("show");

                $(".sdb-table-card").addClass("dimmed");
                $(`.sdb-table-card.sdb-card-${currentMode === 'chuyen' ? 'trong' : 'co-khach'}:not(.selected)`).removeClass("dimmed");
                
                Swal.fire({
                    toast: true, position: 'top-end', showConfirmButton: false, timer: 3000,
                    icon: 'info', title: 'Hãy chọn bàn đích trên sơ đồ'
                });
            });

            $("#btn-cancel-select").click(function() {
                resetPanel();
                if(currentSelectedBan) {
                    setTimeout(() => updatePanel(currentSelectedBan.idBan), 350);
                }
            });

            $("#btn-goi-mon-cu").click(async function() {
                const st = currentSelectedBan.trangThai;
                if (st === 'Có khách') {
                    redirectToGoiMonSecure(currentSelectedBan.idHoaDonHienTai);
                }
                else {
                    const res = await Swal.fire({ title: 'Mở bàn?', text: `Tạo hóa đơn cho Bàn ${currentSelectedBan.soBan}?`, icon: 'info', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#5D4037' });
                    if (res.isConfirmed) {
                        try {
                            const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/createorder/${currentSelectedBan.idBan}`, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${jwtToken}` } });
                            if(!response.ok) throw new Error(await response.text());
                            const data = await response.json();
                            redirectToGoiMonSecure(data.idHoaDon);
                        } catch (err) { Swal.fire('Lỗi', err.message, 'error'); }
                    }
                }
            });

            $("#btn-bao-cao-su-co").click(async function() {
                if (currentSelectedBan.trangThai === "Bảo trì") {
                    const res = await Swal.fire({ title: 'Hủy bảo trì?', text: `Chuyển Bàn ${currentSelectedBan.soBan} về trạng thái trống?`, icon: 'question', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#2E7D32' });
                    if(res.isConfirmed) callApiAction(`reportproblem/${currentSelectedBan.idBan}`, { ghiChuSuCo: "" }, 'Bàn đã sẵn sàng sử dụng!');
                } else {
                    const { value: note } = await Swal.fire({ title: 'Báo cáo sự cố', input: 'text', inputPlaceholder: 'Nhập mô tả sự cố (VD: Hỏng ghế...)', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#D84315' });
                    if (note) callApiAction(`reportproblem/${currentSelectedBan.idBan}`, { ghiChuSuCo: note }, 'Bàn đã chuyển sang bảo trì!');
                }
            });
        });

        $("#btn-tao-don-mang-ve").click(async function() {
            const res = await Swal.fire({
                title: 'Tạo đơn mới?',
                text: `Tạo hóa đơn Tại Quầy / Mang về?`,
                icon: 'info',
                showCancelButton: true,
                confirmButtonColor: '#D84315',
                confirmButtonText: 'Tạo đơn'
            });

            if (res.isConfirmed) {
                try {
                    const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/createorder-no-table`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${jwtToken}` },
                        body: JSON.stringify("Tại quán")
                     });
                    if(!response.ok) throw new Error(await response.text());
                    const data = await response.json();
                    redirectToGoiMonSecure(data.idHoaDon);
                } catch (err) {
                    Swal.fire('Lỗi', err.message, 'error');
                }
            }
        });
    </script>
}

using CafebookModel.Model.ModelWeb.NhanVien;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.DataProtection;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class SoDoBanViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;

        public List<KhuVucWebDto> KhuVucList { get; set; } = new();
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }
        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        private readonly IDataProtector _protector;

        [TempData]
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; set; }

        public SoDoBanViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory, IDataProtectionProvider provider)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
            _protector = provider.CreateProtector("Cafebook.HoaDon.Security");
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnGetAsync()
        {
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken))
            {
                string currentUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString;
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = currentUrl });
            }

            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{httpClient.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/sodobanweb";

            try
            {
                var response = await httpClient.GetFromJsonAsync<List<KhuVucWebDto>>("api/web/nhanvien/sodobanweb/khuvuc-list");
                if (response != null) KhuVucList = response;
            }
            catch (HttpRequestException ex) when (ex.StatusCode == System.Net.HttpStatusCode.Unauthorized)
            {
                HttpContext.Session.Remove("JwtToken");
                TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Phiên đăng nhập hết hạn.";

                string currentUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString;
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = currentUrl });
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                ErrorMessage = "Không thể tải cấu trúc khu vực. Chi tiết: " + ex.Message;
            }

            return Page();
        }

        public IActionResult OnGetEncryptUrl(int id)
        {
            var hash = _protector.Protect(id.ToString());
            return new JsonResult(new { url = $"/nhan-vien/goi-mon/{hash}" });
        }
    }
}

@section Styles {
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/TongQuan.css" asp-append-version="true" />

<div class="tqnv-container fade-in-up">
    <div class="row g-4">

                    <div class="tqnv-badges-container">

                        </span>
                        
                        @if (Model.DashboardData.ThongTin.TrangThaiLamViec == "Đang làm việc")
                        {

                        else

                            <span class="tqnv-badge tqnv-status-inactive">
                                <span class="material-symbols-outlined icon-small">cancel</span>
                                @Model.DashboardData.ThongTin.TrangThaiLamViec
                            </span>
                        }
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="tqnv-profile-details">
                    <div class="tqnv-detail-item">

        $(document).ready(function () {
            $('.modal').appendTo('body');

            var errorMsg = '@Html.Raw(TempData["ErrorMessage"]?.ToString()?.Replace("'", "\\'"))';
            var successMsg = '@Html.Raw(TempData["SuccessMessage"]?.ToString()?.Replace("'", "\\'"))';
            
            if (errorMsg && errorMsg.trim() !== '') {
                Swal.fire({
                    icon: 'error',
                    title: 'Đã xảy ra lỗi',
                    text: errorMsg,
                    confirmButtonColor: '#D84315'
                });
            }

            if (successMsg && successMsg.trim() !== '') {
                Swal.fire({
                    icon: 'success',
                    title: 'Thành công',
                    text: successMsg,
                    confirmButtonColor: '#28a745'
                });
            }
        });
    </script>
}

using CafebookModel.Model.ModelWeb.NhanVien;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication.Cookies;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using System.Net.Http.Headers;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class TongQuanViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;

        public TongQuanViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        public TongQuanDto DashboardData { get; set; } = new();

        [BindProperty]
        public CapNhatThongTinWebDto UpdateModel { get; set; } = new();

        [BindProperty]
        public DoiMatKhauWebDto PasswordModel { get; set; } = new();

        [TempData]
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; set; }

        [TempData]
        public string? SuccessMessage { get; set; }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnGetAsync()
        {
            return await LoadDashboardDataAsync();
        }

        private async Task<IActionResult> LoadDashboardDataAsync()
        {
            var jwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(jwtToken))
            {
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee", new { ReturnUrl = Request.Path + Request.QueryString });
            }

            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            httpClient.DefaultRequestHeaders.Authorization = new AuthenticationHeaderValue("Bearer", jwtToken);

            try
            {
                var response = await httpClient.GetAsync("api/web/nhanvien/TongQuan/dashboard");

                if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                {
                    var data = await response.Content.ReadFromJsonAsync<TongQuanDto>();
                    if (data != null)
                    {
                        DashboardData = data;
                        // Gán sẵn dữ liệu vào form Cập nhật
                        UpdateModel.HoTen = data.ThongTin.HoTen;
                        UpdateModel.SoDienThoai = data.ThongTin.SoDienThoai ?? "";
                        UpdateModel.Email = data.ThongTin.Email;
                        UpdateModel.DiaChi = data.ThongTin.DiaChi;
                    }
                    return Page();
                }

                if (response.StatusCode == System.Net.HttpStatusCode.Unauthorized)
                {
                    await HttpContext.SignOutAsync(CookieAuthenticationDefaults.AuthenticationScheme);
                    HttpContext.Session.Remove("JwtToken");
                    TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Phiên đăng nhập đã hết hạn. Vui lòng đăng nhập lại.";
                    return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee");
                }

                ErrorMessage = "Không thể tải dữ liệu tổng quan.";
                return Page();
            }
            catch (Exception)
            {
                ErrorMessage = "Mất kết nối đến máy chủ API.";
                return Page();
            }
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostUpdateInfoAsync()
        {
            if (!ModelState.IsValid) return await LoadDashboardDataAsync();

            var jwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            httpClient.DefaultRequestHeaders.Authorization = new AuthenticationHeaderValue("Bearer", jwtToken);

            var response = await httpClient.PutAsJsonAsync("api/web/nhanvien/TongQuan/update-info", UpdateModel);
            if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                TempData["SuccessMessage"] = "Cập nhật thông tin thành công!";
                return RedirectToPage();
            }

            TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Cập nhật thông tin thất bại.";
            return await LoadDashboardDataAsync();
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostChangePasswordAsync()
        {
            if (!ModelState.IsValid) return await LoadDashboardDataAsync();

            var jwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            httpClient.DefaultRequestHeaders.Authorization = new AuthenticationHeaderValue("Bearer", jwtToken);

            var response = await httpClient.PostAsJsonAsync("api/web/nhanvien/TongQuan/change-password", PasswordModel);
            if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                TempData["SuccessMessage"] = "Đổi mật khẩu thành công!";
                return RedirectToPage();
            }

            var errorStr = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
            TempData["ErrorMessage"] = string.IsNullOrEmpty(errorStr) ? "Đổi mật khẩu thất bại." : errorStr;
            return await LoadDashboardDataAsync();
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostUploadAvatarAsync(IFormFile avatarFile)
        {
            if (avatarFile == null || avatarFile.Length == 0)
            {
                TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Vui lòng chọn một ảnh.";
                return RedirectToPage();
            }

            var jwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            httpClient.DefaultRequestHeaders.Authorization = new AuthenticationHeaderValue("Bearer", jwtToken);

            using var content = new MultipartFormDataContent();
            using var fileStream = avatarFile.OpenReadStream();
            using var streamContent = new StreamContent(fileStream);
            streamContent.Headers.ContentType = new MediaTypeHeaderValue(avatarFile.ContentType);
            content.Add(streamContent, "avatarFile", avatarFile.FileName);

            var response = await httpClient.PostAsync("api/web/nhanvien/TongQuan/upload-avatar", content);
            if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                TempData["SuccessMessage"] = "Tải ảnh đại diện thành công!";
            }
            else
            {
                TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Tải ảnh lên thất bại.";
            }

            return RedirectToPage();
        }
    }
}
