                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined">local_cafe</span>
                    <div>
                        <h6 class="mb-0 fw-bold">AI Cafebook</h6>
                        <small style="font-size: 0.75rem; opacity: 0.9;">Luôn sẵn sàng hỗ trợ</small>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <button type="button" id="close-chat-popup" class="btn-close btn-close-white" style="font-size: 0.8rem;"></button>
            </div>
            <div class="chat-popup-body" id="popup-chat-history"></div>
            <form id="popupChatForm" class="chat-popup-footer">
                <input type="hidden" id="PopupGuestSessionId" value="@guestSessionId" />
                <input type="text" id="popupChatMessageInput" class="popup-input" placeholder="Nhập câu hỏi..." autocomplete="off" required />
                <button type="submit" id="popupSendButton" class="popup-btn">
                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined">send</span>
                </button>
            </form>
        </div>

        <script>
            $(document).ready(function () {
                const apiBaseUrl = '@apiBaseUrl';
                const guestSessionId = $('#PopupGuestSessionId').val();
                
                const isKhachHang = @isKhachHang.ToString().ToLower();
                const jwtToken = '@(HttpContextAccessor.HttpContext?.Session.GetString("JwtToken") ?? "")';
                const idKhach = '@(User.FindFirstValue(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier) ?? "")';

                let currentSessionId = guestSessionId;
                if (isKhachHang) {
                    currentSessionId = localStorage.getItem('cf_kh_session_' + idKhach) || guestSessionId;
                }

                // CẤU HÌNH API ĐỘNG TÙY TRẠNG THÁI LOGIN (ĐÍNH KÈM TOKEN NẾU LOGIN)
                const chatHeaders = (isKhachHang && jwtToken)
                    ? { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + jwtToken }
                    : { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };

                const historyUrl = isKhachHang
                    ? `${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/khachhang/hotro/history?sessionId=${currentSessionId}`
                    : `${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/guest/hotro/history?guestSessionId=${currentSessionId}`;

                const sendUrl = isKhachHang
                    ? `${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/khachhang/hotro/send`
                    : `${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/guest/hotro/send`;

                // SIGNALR CHO POPUP (NẾU ĐÃ ĐĂNG NHẬP & CHAT VỚI NHÂN VIÊN)
                let isRealtimeModePopup = false;
                let currentIdThongBaoPopup = null;
                let hubConnectionPopup = null;

                const $floatingBtn = $('#cafebook-floating-chat');
                const $popup = $('#cafebook-chat-popup');
                const $toggleBtn = $('#toggle-chat-popup');
                const $closeBtn = $('#close-chat-popup');
                const $badge = $('.chat-badge');

                // Toggle Popup
                $toggleBtn.on('click', function () {
                    $popup.fadeToggle(200); 
                    const isVisible = $popup.is(':visible');
                    localStorage.setItem('isChatPopupOpen', isVisible);
                    if (isVisible) {
                        $badge.hide();
                        scrollToBottomPopup();
                        $('#popupChatMessageInput').focus();
                    }
                });

                $closeBtn.on('click', function () {
                    $popup.fadeOut(200);
                    localStorage.setItem('isChatPopupOpen', 'false');
                });

                // Vẽ tin nhắn UI
                function drawPopupMessage(msg, isUser, isStaff = false) {
                    const type = isUser ? 'user' : (isStaff ? 'staff' : 'bot');
                    const icon = isUser ? 'person' : (isStaff ? 'support_agent' : 'local_cafe'); 
                    let rawText = msg.noiDung || '';
                    let actionButtonsHtml = '';
                    
                    const buttonRegex = /\[BUTTON:\s*(.*?)\s*\|\s*(.*?)\]/g;
                    let match;
                    while ((match = buttonRegex.exec(rawText)) !== null) {
                        let label = match[1].trim();
                        let link = match[2].trim();
                        actionButtonsHtml += `<a href="${link}" class="htvl-btn-action" style="font-size: 0.8rem; padding: 4px 10px; background: white; border: 1px solid #D84315; border-radius: 12px; color: #D84315; text-decoration: none; display: inline-block; margin-right: 5px; margin-top: 5px;">${label} &rarr;</a>`;
                    }

                    let textContent = rawText.replace(buttonRegex, "").replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>').trim().replace(/\n/g, '<br />');
                    let msgTime = msg.thoiGian ? new Date(msg.thoiGian) : new Date();
                    const time = msgTime.toLocaleTimeString('vi-VN', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
                    let actionContainer = actionButtonsHtml !== '' ? `<div class="mt-1">${actionButtonsHtml}</div>` : '';

                    $('#popup-chat-history').append(`
                        <div class="popup-msg-row ${type}">
                            <div class="popup-avatar ${type}"><span class="material-symbols-outlined">${icon}</span></div>
                            <div class="popup-content">
                                <div class="popup-bubble">${textContent}</div>
                                ${actionContainer}
                                <div class="popup-time">${time}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `);
                    scrollToBottomPopup();
                }

                function showPopupTyping() {
                    $('#popup-chat-history').append(`
                        <div class="popup-msg-row bot" id="popup-typing-row">
                            <div class="popup-avatar bot"><span class="material-symbols-outlined">local_cafe</span></div>
                            <div class="popup-content">
                                <div class="popup-bubble"><div class="typing-indicator"><span></span><span></span><span></span></div></div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `);
                    scrollToBottomPopup();
                }

                function scrollToBottomPopup() {
                    const chatHistory = document.getElementById('popup-chat-history');
                    if (chatHistory) chatHistory.scrollTop = chatHistory.scrollHeight;
                }

                // KHỞI ĐỘNG SIGNALR NẾU ĐƯỢC CHUYỂN TỚI NHÂN VIÊN TRONG POPUP
                async function startSignalRPopup() {
                    if (hubConnectionPopup) return;
                    hubConnectionPopup = new signalR.HubConnectionBuilder().withUrl(apiBaseUrl + "/chatHub").build();
                    hubConnectionPopup.on("ReceiveMessage", msg => {
                        if (msg.loaiTinNhan !== 'KhachHang') {
                            drawPopupMessage(msg, false, msg.loaiTinNhan === 'NhanVien');
                            if (!$popup.is(':visible')) { $badge.show(); }
                        }
                    });
                    await hubConnectionPopup.start();
                    await hubConnectionPopup.invoke("JoinGroup", `khach_${idKhach}`);
                }

                // TẢI LỊCH SỬ VÀ HIỂN THỊ NÚT
                async function loadPopupHistory() {
                    try {
                        const res = await fetch(historyUrl, { headers: chatHeaders });
                        const history = await res.json();
                        $('#popup-chat-history').empty();

                        // CHỈ HIỆN NÚT KHI ĐÃ CÓ LỊCH SỬ CHAT (Dùng chung cho cả Khách vãng lai và Khách hàng)
                        if (history.length > 0) {
                            $floatingBtn.show(); 
            
                            history.forEach(msg => {
                                if (msg.idThongBaoHoTro > 0) currentIdThongBaoPopup = msg.idThongBaoHoTro;
                                drawPopupMessage(msg, msg.loaiTinNhan === 'KhachHang', msg.loaiTinNhan === 'NhanVien');
                            });

                            // Nếu đang có ticket nhân viên -> Bật realtime trên popup luôn
                            if (isKhachHang && currentIdThongBaoPopup) {
                                isRealtimeModePopup = true;
                                startSignalRPopup();
                            }

                            if (localStorage.getItem('isChatPopupOpen') === 'true') {
                                $popup.show();
                                setTimeout(scrollToBottomPopup, 300);
                            }
                        } else {
                            $floatingBtn.hide();
                            localStorage.setItem('isChatPopupOpen', 'false');
                        }
                    } catch(e) { console.error("Lỗi tải chat", e); }
                }

                // GỬI TIN NHẮN TỪ POPUP
                $('#popupChatForm').on('submit', async function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const text = $('#popupChatMessageInput').val().trim();
                    if (!text) return;

                    $('#popupChatMessageInput').val('').prop('disabled', true);
                    $('#popupSendButton').prop('disabled', true);
                    
                    drawPopupMessage({ noiDung: text, thoiGian: new Date() }, true);
                    showPopupTyping();

                    // NHÁNH 1: KHÁCH ĐÃ LOGIN VÀ ĐANG CHAT REALTIME TRONG POPUP
                    if (isKhachHang && isRealtimeModePopup && hubConnectionPopup) {
                        await hubConnectionPopup.invoke("SendMessageFromClient", `khach_${idKhach}`, text, parseInt(idKhach), currentSessionId, parseInt(currentIdThongBaoPopup));
                        $('#popup-typing-row').remove();
                        $('#popupChatMessageInput').prop('disabled', false).focus();
                        $('#popupSendButton').prop('disabled', false);
                    } 
                    // NHÁNH 2: GỬI LÊN API AI (CHUNG CHO CẢ GUEST LẪN KHÁCH ĐÃ LOGIN)
                    else {
                        try {
                            const bodyData = isKhachHang 
                                ? JSON.stringify({ noiDung: text, sessionId: currentSessionId })
                                : JSON.stringify({ noiDung: text, guestSessionId: guestSessionId });

                            const res = await fetch(sendUrl, {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: chatHeaders,
                                body: bodyData
                            });
                            const data = await res.json();
                            $('#popup-typing-row').remove();

                            if (data.tinNhanPhanHoi) {
                                drawPopupMessage(data.tinNhanPhanHoi, false, data.tinNhanPhanHoi.loaiTinNhan === 'NhanVien');
                                $floatingBtn.show();
                                if (!$popup.is(':visible')) { $badge.show(); }
                            }

                            if (isKhachHang && data.daChuyenNhanVien) {
                                currentIdThongBaoPopup = data.idThongBaoHoTro;
                                isRealtimeModePopup = true;
                                startSignalRPopup();
                            }
                        } catch (error) {
                            $('#popup-typing-row').remove();
                            drawPopupMessage({ noiDung: "Lỗi kết nối. Vui lòng thử lại.", thoiGian: new Date() }, false);
                        } finally {
                            $('#popupChatMessageInput').prop('disabled', false).focus();
                            $('#popupSendButton').prop('disabled', false);
                        }
                    }
                });

                // Khởi tạo
                loadPopupHistory();
            });
        </script>
    }

    @await RenderSectionAsync("Scripts", required: false)
</body>
</html>

        $('#employeeSidebar').addClass('show');
        $('#sidebarOverlay').addClass('show');
        });
            
        $('#closeSidebarBtn, #sidebarOverlay').click(function () {
        $('#employeeSidebar').removeClass('show');
        $('#sidebarOverlay').removeClass('show');
        });
        });

        function confirmLogout() {
        Swal.fire({
        title: 'Đăng xuất?',
        text: "Bạn có chắc chắn muốn kết thúc phiên làm việc?",
        icon: 'warning',
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonColor: '#D84315',
        cancelButtonColor: '#8D6E63',
        confirmButtonText: 'Có, Đăng xuất',
        cancelButtonText: 'Hủy bỏ',
        customClass: {
        popup: 'swal-coffee-theme'
        }
        }).then((result) => {
        if (result.isConfirmed) {
        document.getElementById('logoutForm').submit();
        }
        });
        }
    </script>

﻿@using System.Security.Claims
@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http
@using CafebookModel.Utils
@inject Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration.IConfiguration Configuration

<ul class="navbar-nav align-items-center flex-column flex-lg-row w-100 gap-2 justify-content-lg-end">
    @if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true && User.IsInRole("KhachHang"))
    {
        var displayName = User.Claims.FirstOrDefault(c => c.Type == ClaimTypes.GivenName)?.Value;
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(displayName))
        {
            displayName = User.Claims.FirstOrDefault(c => c.Type == ClaimTypes.Name)?.Value ?? "Người dùng";
        }

        var avatarUrl = Context.Session.GetString("AvatarUrl");
        
        string apiBaseUrl = Configuration.GetSection("ApiSettings")["BaseUrl"] ?? Configuration["ApiBaseUrl"] ?? "http://localhost:5202";
        apiBaseUrl = apiBaseUrl.TrimEnd('/');
        var avatarSrc = string.IsNullOrEmpty(avatarUrl)
            ? $"{apiBaseUrl}{HinhAnhPaths.WebDefaultAvatar}"
            : avatarUrl;

        <li class="nav-item dropdown w-100 w-lg-auto text-center text-lg-start mt-2 mt-lg-0">
            <a class="nav-link dropdown-toggle d-inline-flex align-items-center justify-content-center px-3 py-2" href="#" id="navbarDropdown" role="button" data-bs-toggle="dropdown" aria-expanded="false" style="border-radius: 8px; background-color: var(--cf-light-gray); transition: background-color 0.2s;">
                <img src="@avatarSrc" alt="Avatar" class="rounded-circle shadow-sm" style="width: 32px; height: 32px; object-fit: cover; margin-right: 8px;" />
                <span class="fw-bold" style="color: var(--cf-dark-brown);">Chào, @displayName</span>
            </a>
            <ul class="dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-end border-0 shadow mt-2" aria-labelledby="navbarDropdown" style="border-radius: 12px; min-width: 240px;">

                <li>
                    <a class="dropdown-item py-2" asp-page="/Account/TaiKhoanTongQuanView">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-2" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">person</span>
                        Tài khoản của tôi
                    </a>
                </li>
                <li>
                    <a class="dropdown-item py-2" asp-page="/Account/ThongTinCaNhanView">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-2" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">badge</span>
                        Hồ sơ cá nhân
                    </a>
                </li>
                <li>
                    <a class="dropdown-item py-2" asp-page="/Account/DoiMatKhauView">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-2" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">lock</span>
                        Đổi mật khẩu
                    </a>
                </li>

                <li><hr class="dropdown-divider"></li>

                <li>
                    <a class="dropdown-item py-2" asp-page="/Account/LichSuDatBanView">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-2" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">event_list</span>
                        Lịch sử đặt bàn
                    </a>
                </li>
                <li>
                    <a class="dropdown-item py-2" asp-page="/Account/LichSuThueSachView">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-2" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">menu_book</span>
                        Lịch sử thuê sách
                    </a>
                </li>
                <li>
                    <a class="dropdown-item py-2" asp-page="/Account/LichSuDonHangView">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-2" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">receipt_long</span>
                        Lịch sử mua hàng
                    </a>
                </li>

                <li><hr class="dropdown-divider"></li>

                <li>
                    <button type="button" class="dropdown-item text-danger py-2 fw-bold" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#logoutConfirmModal">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-2" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">logout</span>
                        Đăng xuất
                    </button>
                </li>
            </ul>
        </li>
    }
    else
    {
        <li class="nav-item w-100 w-lg-auto mt-3 mt-lg-0">
            <a class="btn btn-outline-primary w-100 text-nowrap" asp-page="/Account/DangKyView" style="text-transform: none; font-size: 1rem; border-width: 2px;">
                Đăng ký
            </a>
        </li>
        <li class="nav-item w-100 w-lg-auto mb-2 mb-lg-0">
            <a class="btn btn-primary w-100 text-nowrap" asp-page="/Account/DangNhapView" style="text-transform: none; font-size: 1rem;">
                Đăng nhập
            </a>
        </li>
    }
</ul>

@if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true && User.IsInRole("KhachHang"))
{

        <div class="modal-dialog modal-dialog-centered">

                        Bạn có chắc chắn muốn đăng xuất khỏi tài khoản của mình không?

                        <button type="button" class="btn btn-outline-secondary fw-bold px-4 py-2 w-100 w-sm-auto" data-bs-dismiss="modal" style="border-radius: 8px; border-width: 2px;">
